Important International News

Disturbances in Egypt Continue

Cairo is Under Extraordinary Guard

Egyptian King Rejects People's Party Petition

Reuters, Poseidon, 22nd - Disturbances broke out here again this afternoon. Mobs attempted to burn down the stables of the Municipal Council. Police were forced to open fire on the crowd, resulting in one death and two injuries. Egyptian troops have rushed to the scene of the disturbances, which are currently confined to areas inhabited by Egyptians and do not involve foreign residential areas.

Reuters, London, 22nd - British Foreign Secretary Henderson stated in the Lower House today that the Egyptian government itself has indicated that there is no need to adopt special protection plans. The British government is well aware of Britain's responsibilities under the declaration to protect the lives and property of foreigners in Egypt.

Reuters, Alexandria, 23rd - According to reliable sources, the petition by the Egyptian National Party to convene a special session of parliament on July 26 has been rejected by the Egyptian King. National Society, London, 22nd - The Cairo correspondent of the Daily News now believes that the Egyptian King has seriously considered abdicating, which would cause the cabinet to resign immediately.

National Society, Cairo, 22nd - Many riots also occurred in various provincial towns last night. Although most have restored order, in Port Said, protesters attempted to set fire to the city-owned stables again and were shot by police, killing two and injuring many. However, the situation is still critical. Currently, all parties are eagerly awaiting the Egyptian King's response to the National Party's request to immediately convene a special session of parliament. Only a few shops are open in Cairo. In the streets, soldiers with rifles and bayonets are constantly patrolling. Machine guns have been set up in front of public buildings and important places. However, according to the prime minister's interview with reporters, the internal situation is not as serious as it appears on the surface. Monday's riots were not revolutionary in nature, as villagers were unwilling to stop working to participate in the demonstrations, resulting in complete failure. It should be known that the Italian-French dispute cannot be resolved by riots.

Japanese Military Council Formally Meets Yesterday

The Draft Reply Was Passed as Originally Proposed

The Government Convenes an Emergency Cabinet Meeting

Finance Minister and Navy Minister Prepare to Resign

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 23rd - The official military council meeting was held in the East Hall of the Imperial Palace at 10:00 this morning. In addition to the council members, Major General Horikawa, Director of the Military Affairs Bureau, also attended as the first head of the Naval General Staff. Marshal Togo took the seat of chairman and announced the opening of the meeting. First, General Taniguchi, Chief of the Naval General Staff, explained the draft proposal consulted at the Hayama Imperial Villa yesterday afternoon. Then, the formal review began. Each council member stated their opinions, which were recorded. At 10:40, the original proposal was passed and the meeting adjourned. Marshal Togo and the other council members retired to a separate room and were given lunch. Marshal Togo and General Taniguchi left for Tokyo Station at 2:22 p.m. to serve at the Hayama Imperial Villa to report the results of the meeting. Thus, the opinion of the Navy, that defense defects are difficult to remedy, eventually reached the Emperor's ears, making the political situation even more significant.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 23rd - At the informal council meeting, Finance Minister Zaibu had no choice but to follow the Navy's consistent practice of supporting Marshal Togo's proposal and acknowledging the naval power strength in the London Treaty he signed.

There are indeed defects, so the resignation of Finance Minister Zaibu is only a matter of time. However, the government has decided to support Finance Minister Zaibu and fight with the Privy Council from beginning to end to proceed with the procedures for requesting approval. However, among the elders of the Navy, it is said that Finance Minister Zaibu clearly stated before departing for the London Conference that he would absolutely adhere to the three major principles. After returning to the country, he repeatedly changed the Chief of the Naval General Staff, causing an unprecedented conflict within the Navy. Most of them believe that he should resign to take responsibility for the internal disunity. As a result, Finance Minister Zaibu will resign after the Privy Council consults and requests approval or after the treaty is ratified.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 23rd - The Navy's claim that defense defects are difficult to remedy was formally passed as originally proposed at today's military council meeting. The government decided to take the final step, which is to consult the Privy Council on the arms reduction treaty. An emergency cabinet meeting was convened this afternoon to decide on all procedures.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 23rd - The content of the military council's reply is extremely secret. It is said that the main idea is: "The naval power strength under the London Treaty has defects in wartime use and is extremely difficult to fully remedy." It also adds: "Japan's minimum level of defense power must be thoroughly implemented." The military said that when drafting the reply, they did not participate in any political significance, only stating what they believed. The interpretation is left to the government or the Privy Council's discretion.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 23rd - The Japanese government, after holding an emergency cabinet meeting at 2:00 p.m. today, immediately proceeded with the procedures for consulting the Privy Council in writing. Therefore, the situation has shifted from the military to the Privy Council. There will be more waves in the future, but ratification is expected to occur by September at the latest. However, the real difficulty for the government will remain after the treaty is established, namely, the relationship between the surplus from arms reduction and tax cuts. Because Finance Minister Zaibu was in an isolated and helpless position at the council meeting regarding supplementing defense defects, the government held a summit meeting at the Prime Minister's residence on the afternoon of the 21st to discuss how to escape this predicament. It was decided that the government would listen to the Navy's demands regarding supplementing defense defects, that is, sending General Taniguchi, Chief of the Naval General Staff, to visit Marshal Togo to convey the government's opinion. Togo said that the government's opinion could not be counted on. Please provide concrete evidence from the Prime Minister. It is said that the Japanese government has given the Navy written evidence to serve as proof for future use. The government recently stated that the surplus will be incorporated into the sixth-year budget, and it is feared that there will not be much money. This seems to be due to this. One of the purposes of arms reduction is to reduce the burden on the people. If it is like this, it is truly unnecessary.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 23rd - Prime Minister Hamaguchi, based on the decision of today's emergency cabinet meeting, is scheduled to leave Tokyo at 8:00 a.m. on the 24th to visit the Hayama Imperial Villa to meet the Emperor, to request consultation with the Privy Council on the London Naval Treaty, and to report in detail on the progress made so far.

Reuters, Tokyo, 23rd - The Japanese government's actions on ratifying the London Naval Treaty, which had been sluggish for a long time, have resumed today. This is partly because the United States has already ratified the treaty, and partly because the long-standing dispute over the treaty among naval leaders has ended through compromise. After the cabinet meeting this afternoon, authorities announced that Prime Minister Hamaguchi will travel to the Hayama Imperial Villa tomorrow to meet the Emperor and request approval of the treaty, which will then be submitted to the Privy Council for review. The discussion by the Privy Council is expected to take several weeks, but it is expected that the treaty will eventually be passed. The slowness of the proceedings in recent weeks has been entirely due to the inability of key naval personnel to agree on a memorial to the Emperor on the treaty's impact on national defense. This morning, naval personnel from the Supreme Military Council gathered at the Imperial Palace in Tokyo to discuss and resolve the dispute between the two factions. One faction, led by Kato and Togo, was vehemently opposed to ratifying the treaty, while the other faction, led by Navy Minister Zaibu, advocated unconditional ratification. Now, a compromise has been reached on the opinions of the two factions. Although its content has not yet been announced, it is understood that due to the treaty's restrictive conditions, Japan's national defense is exposed to loopholes. Therefore, it is planned to remedy this by expanding the air force and other methods. Moreover, with the treaty limited to six years, it is possible to avoid major insurance risks by ratifying it today. However, it is declared that in the next naval conference, Japan must resolutely demand a ratio of 70 percent for all types of warships. Although this compromise is a political setback for the government, it will not cause a cabinet upheaval. If so, the treaty will be difficult to ratify. It is widely believed that after the treaty is ratified, Navy Minister Zaibu may be forced to resign.

US President Formally Signs the London Naval Treaty

Congressmen Flock to Summer Resorts

Newspaper Editorials Hold Divergent Views

National Society, Washington, 22nd - President Hoover formally signed the London Naval Treaty at 3:01 p.m. today in the East Room of the White House. The ceremony was simple. All US representatives who attended the naval conference, including Stimson, Adams, Robinson, and Reed, were present. In addition, Vice President Curtis and several senators were also present. The weather has been unusually hot in recent days, and the senators who have been participating in special meetings every day have been suffering greatly. Therefore, as soon as yesterday's special meeting adjourned, the congressmen packed their bags and went to various summer resorts. It is said that if it were not for the recent heat wave, the passage of the treaty would not have been so smooth. Newspapers are still divided into two factions: supporters and opponents. The opponents continue to attack the treaty without slackening. Newspapers calling themselves the "Big Navy Faction" are filled with criticisms of the treaty, saying that it will not have good results in the future. And a group of newspapers that extremely advocate limiting naval preparations fear that the treaty cannot achieve actual naval restrictions. Other newspapers that support the treaty say that the passage of the treaty is a legitimate step. Even if it cannot be fully achieved at once, it at least proves that Americans are inclined to international thought. Some people are worried that Japan's naval buildup will increase and the United States will abandon its fortification rights in the Pacific, but they are few in number and therefore not taken seriously.

Reuters, London, 22nd - British Prime Minister MacDonald, referring to the US Senate's passage of the London Naval Treaty yesterday by a vote of 58 to 4, said in the Lower House today that, in light of the circumstances, the second reading of the British Naval Treaty should proceed immediately in order to realize it as soon as possible and should not be delayed until the fall. According to the schedule, the current session of Congress will end at the end of this month, but the British Prime Minister believes that the consideration of the second reading of this bill will not take much time. Reuters, Washington, 22nd - US President Hoover signed the London Naval Treaty this afternoon. The US President said that after other governments ratify the treaty, it will transform a sentiment held in the hearts of billions of people into a practical covenant of government and international relations, and will make the world re-trust the moral power of goodwill and patient negotiation, and not trust the blind power of suspicion and armed competition. The treaty can also safeguard the United States' complete defense.

US President Concerned About Income Tax

National Society, 22nd - According to today's news, President Hoover is deeply concerned about the future increase in income tax. Mr. Hoover is currently advocating that all government agencies cooperate to reduce expenses in order to have a surplus of US$100,000,000 to make up for the historical deficit. If an increase in income tax suddenly occurs at this time, it will make his plan to reduce government expenses even more difficult. According to Treasury Secretary Mellon, no matter how much the government tries to economize, an increase in income tax will likely be unavoidable when the current fiscal year ends. What is now being worried about is that this move will greatly disappoint the public. Mr. Hoover is now urging all cabinet members to plan ways to ensure that each department can achieve the lowest level of thrift.

US Republican Party Undertakes Reorganization

National Society, Washington, 22nd - Republican leaders today undertook reorganization to prepare for the autumn parliamentary election campaign. Senator Moses will be in charge of party affairs east of the Mississippi River, while Senator Steiwer will be responsible for propaganda in both departments. The party's reorganization this time proves that it is aware that only those familiar with local conditions can handle affairs. After the passage of the new tariff law, leaders from the agricultural states in both departments have expressed dissatisfaction. The party's move is largely aimed at addressing this issue.

Japanese Minseito Party Lobbies the Entire Country

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 23rd - In order to counter the Seiyukai Party's large-scale lobbying, the Minseito Party has agreed on a lobbying network for the entire country. The detailed plan was finalized yesterday. All the general affairs officers and all the staff members will be dispatched to lobby. All cabinet members from the Hamaguchi Prime Minister's party will stand at the forefront. The places where the speeches will be given range from Hokkaido in the north to Kyushu in the south. Prime Minister Hamaguchi will also appear at the Kanto and Kansai conferences held in Tokyo and Osaka to give a major speech.

Tragedy Amidst Celebrations in Rhineland

Reuters, Koblenz, 22nd - A tragedy occurred during the celebrations of the withdrawal of foreign troops from the Rhineland. Tonight, there was a fireworks display in this area to welcome President Hindenburg's visit. Late at night, viewers were returning home and crossing a floating bridge when the bridge suddenly collapsed, causing hundreds of people to fall into the river. In the darkness, many who struggled in the water perished. Twenty-four bodies have now been recovered.

Reuters, Berlin, 23rd - The police chief of Koblenz has ordered the cessation of all celebrations due to the bridge collapse. President Hindenburg has also suspended his tour of other places and is staying there to participate in the memorial service.

Earthquake Occurs in Southern Italy

Reuters, Rome, 23rd - According to news from Rome, an earthquake occurred in southern Italy, killing nineteen people and injuring ten. Details are not yet known.

Reuters, Rome, 23rd - There were severe earthquakes in Naples and throughout the province of Catania this morning, occurring intermittently. Part of the Naples Palace collapsed, killing two and injuring five. A subsequent telegram said that it has now been ascertained that more than one hundred and fifty people have died and many more have been injured in the earthquake. One hundred people were killed or injured in the town of Melfi near Naples.

British King Agrees to Hold Round Table Conference

Reuters, London, 22nd - It is heard that the British King has agreed to hold a round table conference at St. James's Palace to resolve the Indian issue. The London Naval Conference, in which five countries participated, was held in this palace a few months ago.

Universal Parliamentary Union Closes

Reuters, London, 22nd - The 26th Universal Parliamentary Union Conference, which opened on the 16th of this month, closed today. The government held a banquet to say goodbye to the 600 participants, including representatives from the parliaments of 31 countries, chaired by Justice Minister Sankey.

French Authorities Prevent Strike Wave

National Society, Paris, 22nd - After the metalworkers' strike in Lille, France, their leader threatened a general strike on Wednesday. It is now expected that textile workers will join. The authorities have dispatched a large number of police to various suburbs of Lille to prevent conflicts. The current labor unrest was caused by opposition to the wage cuts in the newly promulgated social service regulations. The workers demand that unemployment insurance and medical expenses be borne by the employers, and not, as at present, be deducted from the workers' wages.

Torrential Rain in New York Reduces Heat

Reuters, New York, 22nd - The temperature in New York was very high yesterday. At least twenty people died of heatstroke, and no fewer than twenty horses collapsed on the road. But this afternoon, torrential rain poured down and the heat has been reduced.

Soviet Russia Approves Chicherin's Resignation

National Society, Moscow, 22nd - Soviet Russian People's Commissar for Foreign Affairs Chicherin has been on sick leave for a long time. The Russian government has now approved his resignation and has promoted Deputy People's Commissar Litvinov to fill the vacancy.

Irish Road Workers' General Strike

National Society, Dublin, 22nd - Irish railway workers began a general strike yesterday at midnight. 12,000 have joined and it is still not sure if the rest will join.

Flood in Turkestan

National Society, Moscow, 22nd - The flood in Turkestan within Russia is so severe that it has never been seen before. Traffic is completely blocked, thousands are homeless, and material losses are enormous. It is reported that a section of the newly built Turkestan-Siberia Railway has also been washed away.

Public Telegram

Telegram from Manila to Shen Bao Newspaper, forwarded to the Central Party Headquarters, Party Headquarters in all provinces, organizations, and newspapers: Gao Weiguo, a notorious bandit from Quanzhou, who changed his name to Gao Jingli, is extremely fierce and has been the source of much resentment. However, Lin Shouguo, the naval brigade commander, actually recruited him and obtained recognition from the authorities. The people are already extremely frightened. Recently, he was even ordered to take over the defense of Quanzhou, making a notorious bandit of more than ten years the military and political leader of a county. As a result, the bandit's ferocity has become even more rampant, and the plundering and killing have become even more unbridled. The people's self-defense corps resulted in an unprecedented massacre of the city. Hundreds of innocent people have been killed, and property losses are incalculable. Burning and killing is still continuing. Many overseas Chinese in the Philippines are from Quanzhou. Urgent news reports have caused cries of grief. At today's overseas Chinese conference, public sentiment is agitated. We think that Quanzhou is not an uncivilized area, and the people of Quanzhou are also Chinese citizens. However, the so-called formal naval and marine corps are allowed to wantonly massacre and sacrifice the lives and property of the people. Hundreds of thousands of overseas Chinese drifting in foreign countries are constantly worried about not having a home to return to. In addition to telegraphing the government and military authorities to appeal, we ask for assistance. We are extremely hopeful. Chen Yinglai, Li Cuiquan, Yang Kongying, Xue Minlao, of the Presidium of the Overseas Chinese Conference in the Philippines, kowtow.

Important News

He Yingqin Will Go to the Front to Supervise the Troops

Hankou Correspondence: He Yingqin, Director of the Wuhan Headquarters, took a plane from Hankou to Luohe the other day to discuss operational strategies for the Pinghan Railway line with He Chengjiong, Commander-in-Chief of the Third Army Corps. The plan for attacking Xuchang and Zhengzhou has been largely decided. They then went together to Guide to visit General Chiang. After visiting General Chiang, He Chengjiong immediately returned to Luohe to make arrangements, while He Yingqin went to Bozhou to speak to the besieging armies, and then returned to the front to meet with General Chiang. At six o'clock in the morning on the 22nd, he took a plane back to Hankou from there, with Zhang Yougu, the captain of the First Aviation Team, piloting himself. The plane arrived safely at the Hankou airfield at noon that day. Qian Dajun, He Guoguang, Wu Xingya, Liu Wendao, and other important staff members of the Headquarters came to the airfield to welcome him. After getting off the plane, He Yingqin took a car to the Headquarters and then returned to his private residence to rest. I visited Mr. He at the Headquarters and Mr. He said, "I went to Luohe this time to discuss the plan to attack Xuchang and Zhengzhou with Commander-in-Chief He. After the decision was made, we took a plane to the front together to visit General Chiang and presented everything to General Chiang. General Chiang has adopted this plan and ordered it to be implemented as soon as possible. Commander-in-Chief He then returned to Luohe to make arrangements, while I went to Bozhou to inspect the besieging soldiers, who were extremely brave. Sun Ni's remnants can be completely eliminated. After the inspection, I returned to Hankou from the front. I also took the opportunity to inspect the Pinghan line. The enemy's counterattack on Luo and Yan failed and they retreated in disarray to the north of Linying. There is no trace of the rebel army in the villages around Luobei. When the general attack order is issued again, the entire rebel army on the line can be completely resolved. After returning to Hankou, I will make some arrangements and then go to the front to supervise the troops." (July 22nd)

Dramatic Increase in Wuhan's Population

Over 700,000 Refugees Seek Shelter in the Provincial Capital

Soaring Cost of Living Leaves Many Commoners Destitute and Displaced

Hankou Communication: Wuhan's original population of over two million residents, with its numerous factories and flourishing markets, has recently experienced an influx of people due to the Communist bandit troubles in the interior of Hubei Province. Most residents from various counties with even modest assets have relocated to Wuhan to escape the red flames. According to recent household registration statistics from the Municipal Government's Public Security Bureau, the provincial capital's population has increased by over 700,000 in the past few months. Consequently, landlords, seeing the surge in population and shortage of housing, are colluding to manipulate and increase rents. Some are forcing existing tenants to move out, only to re-rent the premises at exorbitant prices. Others are forcibly abandoning the solar calendar, demanding extra rent payments, or hoarding multiple properties for subletting, with individuals becoming "second landlords" and profiting in the process. Residents of Wuhan are in a state of panic, and tenant associations have repeatedly petitioned the provincial government and various provincial and municipal party headquarters, requesting them to direct the Public Security Bureau and the Social Affairs Bureau to strictly crack down on these practices to protect the housing of the common people. The Public Security and Social Affairs Bureaus recently jointly issued a public notice, stating that they would uniformly crack down on and strictly investigate any increases in rent or the use of the lunar calendar for rent calculation. However, the exorbitant rents remain unchanged, mainly due to the shortage of housing and the overcrowding of people with nowhere to live. As a result, current housing prices are more than double those in Beijing and Shanghai, and the future trend remains uncertain. As for rice, the daily consumption for the Wuhan area is estimated to be around 10,000 *shi* (approximately 1,400,000 kilograms). However, rice-producing regions in Hubei Province are plagued by bandits, and transportation is disrupted. The bulk of the grain supply is currently being transported to Wuhan from Sichuan and Shanghai. However, the daily demand is enormous, and the supply is difficult to secure, leading merchants to hoard and speculate, causing rice prices to skyrocket. Recently, the price per *shi* (approximately 140 *jin*, or 70 kilograms) has reached twenty yuan, with a continued upward trend. For a family of several members, even just the expenses for housing and rice are difficult to manage, not to mention other necessities. The prices of all goods are rising, leading many impoverished people to beg for alms daily, filling the roads and sleeping in the streets. Driven to desperation by the hardships of life, there are daily reports of people committing suicide by drowning themselves in the river. For example, Wu Chengjin, formerly the head of the Shashi Anti-Smoking Bureau and a native of Echeng, who resided in Yanzhishan in Wuchang, recently committed suicide by hanging himself after being unable to make ends meet. Yesterday, he and his wife first threw their two children, aged five and three, into the river, and then hanged themselves. The entire family of four perished, a truly tragic situation. (July 21st)

Joint Hunan-Jiangxi Campaign to Suppress Huang Gonglue

Liu Jianxu's Troops Stationed in Western Jiangxi

Nanchang Communication: The counties of Pingxiang, Lianhua, Yongxin, and Ninggang in western Jiangxi, bordering Ling, Cha, Li, and You in eastern Hunan, have long been areas where Communist bandits operate. Since last year, the counties of Ninggang and Yongxin have been occupied by bandits led by Yuan Wencai, Wang Zuo, and Liu Zuoshu, plunging the area into darkness. Recently, Huang Gonglue led over 10,000 bandits, equipped with thousands of rifles, mortars, and machine guns, to attack Ji'an from Anfu and Lianhua on the 20th (this was the third such attack). Fortunately, Deng Ying's division defended the city while urgently requesting assistance from Zhang Huizan via telegram. Upon receiving the telegram, Zhang ordered the 52nd Brigade to advance from Xia towards Jishui to provide reinforcements. The combined forces successfully repelled the Huang bandits, and Ji'an was spared from danger. However, the border defense line between Jiangxi and Hunan is too long, and there are too many bandits, making troop allocation difficult. Lu Diping, the commander-in-chief of the Ninth Route Army, believing that the situation in Hunan had been stabilized, specifically requested He Jian via telegram to dispatch troops to western Jiangxi to jointly suppress the Huang bandits. Lu soon received a reply telegram from He Xiaowu, stating that in addition to the one battalion already sent to Jiangxi, another regiment from Liu Jianxu's division would be stationed in Pingxiang to conduct guerrilla warfare, which would further strengthen the defense of Pingxiang. Furthermore, according to news from the Ninth Route Army headquarters, He Jian, in order to eradicate the Communist bandits on the Hunan-Jiangxi border within a specific timeframe, specifically appointed Wei Zhongsu as the commander of bandit suppression in eastern Hunan, coordinating closely with the Ninth Route Army in western Jiangxi. In addition to sending Huang Xingyi and Zhang Huan as representatives to Hunan to discuss all joint suppression plans with Chairman He, Lu and Zhang have also dispatched Deng Weishan, the director of the Municipal Affairs Bureau, as a representative to Pingxiang to transfer to Hunan and liaise with Commander Wei on methods to jointly suppress the Communist bandits in western Jiangxi and to handle coordination matters. Deng departed yesterday. Furthermore, Wang Yinxi, the director of the Department of Civil Affairs, departed from the province yesterday to inspect the disaster situation in western Jiangxi and to organize guard teams and local defense in Shanggao, Yifeng, and other counties. (July 21st)

Chu Lai and Other Counties Launch "Purification of the Countryside"

Bengbu Communication: In the area of Chu County, Lai'an County, and other counties in northern Anhui, the local people have been suffering greatly in recent months due to the disturbances caused by the bandit Jiang Guochang. Although the police and local militias have repeatedly suppressed the bandits, they return as soon as the troops leave, failing to achieve fundamental eradication. Since the beginning of this month, after Zhang Lisheng, the commander of the Second Cavalry Division, personally supervised the suppression in Chu County, all major bandit gangs in Zilaiqiao, Lao Jiashan, Gaoshanji, and other places have been successively defeated and are almost completely wiped out. Commander Zhang believes that there are still scattered bandit gangs near Chu County and that only by launching a "purification of the countryside" can their roots be completely eradicated. In addition to dispatching troops to pursue and suppress the bandits in coordination with local militia police, he specifically telegraphed Commander-in-Chief Jiang, requesting him to order the Anhui provincial government to instruct the six counties of Chu County, Lai'an County, Quanjiao County, Chuzhou County, Tianchang County, and Dingyuan County to launch the "purification of the countryside" to eliminate the source of bandits and prevent future troubles. Upon receiving the telegram, Jiang immediately instructed Ma Fuxiang, the chairman of the Anhui provincial government, via telegram, to order the six counties of Chu County, Lai'an County, etc., to immediately launch the "purification of the countryside." The Anhui provincial government promptly issued orders for each county to implement the plan. Commander-in-Chief Jiang believes that Zhang Lisheng has been exceptionally effective in suppressing bandits and consolidating the rear in the area of Chu County, and in addition to sending a telegram of commendation, he has also appointed Zhang as the concurrent commander of the Jinpu Railway protection between Pukou and Bengbu. After accepting the appointment, Zhang officially took office in Bengbu and dispatched his chief of staff, Sun Baoyu, to Beijing to seek instructions from headquarters. The Railway Protection Command was formally established yesterday, and its internal organization has been completed. (July 21st)

Suzhou County Finance Bureau Reorganized as Finance Bureau

Organizational Regulations Approved by the Provincial Government

The finance bureaus in the counties of Jiangsu Province have now been reorganized as finance bureaus. The organizational regulations have been approved by the provincial government and are recorded below: (Article 1) In accordance with Article 16 of the County Magistrate Organization Law, each county government in this province shall establish a finance bureau. (Article 2) The county finance bureau shall be responsible for matters such as tax collection, bond issuance, management of public property, and other local finance matters. (Article 3) The county finance bureau shall have one director, who shall be subject to the direction and supervision of the Department of Finance, oversee the overall affairs of the bureau, and direct and supervise subordinate staff. (Article 4) The county finance bureau shall be divided into one or three sections, each with one section chief, who shall, under the director's orders, handle the affairs under their jurisdiction. One to three staff members and three to four clerks shall be appointed to assist the director and handle bureau affairs under the orders of their superiors. (Article 5) The county finance bureau director shall be selected by the county magistrate from two or three qualified candidates based on examination results and submitted to the Department of Finance for review and appointment by the provincial government. However, before the examination is implemented, the original procedures may be followed. Section chiefs shall be selected by the bureau director and submitted to the county government for approval and appointment by the Department of Finance. Staff members shall be selected by the bureau director and submitted to the county government for appointment and filed with the Department of Finance. (Article 6) The detailed rules for the county finance bureau shall be drafted by the finance bureau and submitted to the Department of Finance for filing. (Article 7) The county finance bureau may establish a finance discussion committee, the regulations for which shall be separately determined.

The Course of Banditry in Jiande County, Zhejiang Province

Jiande County, Zhejiang Province, is a key route on the upper reaches of the Qiantang River. On the 6th of this month, a large band of Communist bandits disturbed the Yangweibu area, 15 *li* from the county seat in the southern countryside. With limited military and police strength to resist, the entire town of Yangweibu was looted, and local gentry Hu Zhiyan, Xie Baohui, and Xie Baochun were brutally murdered. The entire county was shocked. The city only had one company of security guards stationed there, which could only defend itself. Therefore, wealthy households near the city walls fled to Hangzhou. At the same time, Sandu town in the eastern countryside of the county was also burned and looted, and the villages of Licai, Yougao, and Louxia in the southern countryside were also successively burned. After the Second Battalion of the Third Security Regiment arrived, they consulted with the water police to suppress smuggling.

Page 8

After jointly encircling and suppressing the bandits, over thirty people were captured, and the bandit momentum was slightly reduced. However, over a hundred bandits were discovered again in Yangxi town in the western countryside, and houses were burned in the Guocun area, 15 *li* away. They also infiltrated the border of Chun'an County, looting the entire town of Chayuan, and their momentum was very strong. Subsequently, Zhu Mingtao, the commander of the Third Regiment of the Security Team, led a team to Jiande to direct the encirclement and suppression. After successively capturing many key criminals, and after a thorough investigation, the ringleaders were executed on the spot, including Tong Yunjiao, the pseudo-deputy commander's sister (in her twenties, she was the bandits' military judge, and the locals who were killed by the bandits were all tried by her), and the Communist father Tong Bichen. The remaining bandits have also been executed. Therefore, the bandit momentum in the county has now calmed down somewhat. However, there are still bandit traces appearing in the border areas of Chun'an, Pujiang, Suian, and other counties near Jiande.

Liu Jianxu's Proposals for the Aftermath in Southern Hunan

Changsha Communication: After the remnants of Zhang Guiji's troops fled back to Guangxi, the Fourth Route Army, in addition to dispatching the Li and Chen brigades to Guangxi to pursue them, has redeployed the remaining troops back to Hunan Province, dividing up areas to eradicate and suppress the Communist bandits. However, the twenty-plus counties in southern Hunan border Guangdong and Guangxi, and the people are fiercely independent. After the troops of the Gui and Zhang factions rampaged back and forth, and after several major battles, the local area has suffered greatly. Moreover, there are scattered soldiers and weapons everywhere, and looting is frequently heard. Liu Jianxu, believing that his department is stationed in the area and cannot shirk responsibility, listed four points based on his observations and set out from Hengzhou on the 17th, arriving in the province by car at 1:00 PM. He immediately met with He Jian to explain everything in detail. He praised him greatly and assigned the matters to the Countryside Purification Command and the Department of Civil Affairs for proper handling. The following are Liu Jianxu's proposals: "Commander-in-Chief He Junjian, the counties in southern Hunan border Guangdong and Guangxi, and have always borne the brunt of the campaigns against Gui and Zhang. This time, the remnants ravaged the area, leaving it utterly devastated, with cries of sorrow echoing everywhere, a scene of devastation. I have been stationed here for a long time and am deeply concerned. Seeing this tragic state, I cannot bear to sit idly by. Therefore, I specifically list several points for your inspection and review. Many county magistrates and deputy directors of household defense in southern Hunan have been diligent in their duties, but there are also many who hold sinecures and take advantage of opportunities to support the rebels. People are talking and public opinion is in an uproar. Therefore, I request that careful selection of personnel be made, that the local defense be reorganized, and that those who supported the rebels be punished according to the severity of their offenses. The establishment of area commands was originally intended to consolidate forces for suppression and facilitate command. The method was good and has achieved some success. Now, because the rebel army invaded Hunan, it has been effectively suspended, and the Communist bandits are jumping around, like a fire growing hotter. If we do not take early precautions, the future banditry may be even worse than the current situation in Pingjiang, Liuyang, and Yueyang. Therefore, I request that you issue a clear order to restore the command and set a deadline for the start of suppression efforts. When the rebel army collapsed, many weapons were scattered, resulting in a surge in gun collection, with many names and a lack of unified methods. There are also no standardized orders. As a result, the civilians who possess weapons do not know what to do, so they hide them and do not report them. The personnel collecting weapons engage in various corrupt practices, such as fraud and theft. Even large numbers of weapons are collected and incorporated, but without any effectiveness. The result is that it creates an opportunity for the Communist bandits to lure them, giving tigers wings, which is a terrible potential threat. Therefore, I request that personnel be dispatched to coordinate the suppression and pacification to achieve unification. The people have suffered countless tangible and intangible losses in the areas ravaged by the rebel army. Some have been killed by stray bullets, some have had their houses destroyed, and some have had their entire livelihood destroyed. Those who survived the looting are crying and waiting to be fed. Therefore, I request that personnel be dispatched to investigate and provide relief, especially to those who are in need. The four points above are all urgent tasks for the counties in southern Hunan. I have seen the suffering of the people and dare not conceal it. I have presumptuously submitted this report to appeal on behalf of the people. Please review and make a decision. Respectfully submitted by Liu Jianxu."

Soviet Russia Directs the International Communist Party's Propaganda Plan

Nine Items Decided at Recent Meeting

Offensive Launched Toward the Northeast

Harbin Communication: Soviet Russia's policy of communist infiltration in the Northeast, according to its planned schedule, has decided to utilize the International Communist Party as its vanguard. The consulates stationed in various locations in the Northeast, supported by the financial resources of the East China Railway and the Far Eastern Bank, are sparing no expense to buy off Chinese, Korean, and Japanese youths for their work. The communist cases that flourished for a time in the Northeast this year are clear evidence of this. Therefore, the authorities are not daring to relax their vigilance in preventing these activities. A radical communist manifesto was recently discovered in the city, and after a thorough search by the police authorities, Yu Ergui, the leader of the communists who was on the run, was arrested. Yu was formerly the principal of the Eighth Middle School and a mainstay of the Communist Party in the Northeast. After being arrested, he was escorted to Liaoning to be tried together with those arrested in Shenyang in the previous case. As a result of Yu's arrest, the Soviet Russian-directed International Communist Party plan, which has already been discussed, has become clear. The International Communist Party recently convened a conference near the capital of Jilin Province. Soviet Russian consulate personnel mostly participated in the discussion. The attending representatives were divided into the Harbin district representative, the Yilan district representative, the Yanji district representative, the Korean Communist Party Manchuria section, the East Manchuria Railway cadre organization committee, the education branch organization committee, the North Manchuria Youth General Alliance representative, and the East Manchuria Youth General Alliance representative. The following matters were decided: (1) The International Communist Party will issue a declaration to participate in the revolutionary movement in order to achieve unified cooperation. (2) The International Communist Party will maintain its previous pace of cooperation and maintain contact with each other. (3) The International Communist Party will implement the destruction of all Japanese facilities and agencies in Manchuria and Mongolia. (4) Act according to plan. All weapons and supplies necessary for assassinations should be obtained from Soviet Russian agencies in the area. (5) In order to understand the state of affairs of each party, a report must be submitted at least once a month to exchange information. (6) For the sake of unified methods, the International Communist Party will implement the education of Soviet Russian citizens and the training of assassination movements after a meeting. (7) The International Communist Party must seek methods to facilitate the conduct of business. (8) The International Communist Party and its affiliated groups must formulate a secret code of identification for their members. (9) The International Communist Party must first point out the crimes of its enemies, destroy them, or create terror by agile methods. (15th)

Local News

Songjiang

The Donghui Charity Association Invites Directors: The directors of the Old Songshu Seven County Charity Association, organized by the Benxian San Shan Hall, have a term of office set at three years. The county magistrate of the location serves as supervisor, and each county magistrate is permitted to recommend appointments. It has been learned that the terms of office of the directors of Songyi County, Chen Zongzhen, Zhu Shijin, Zhang Fusun, and Hu Deliang, have expired, and County Magistrate Jin has prepared a letter to reappoint them for another term. The terms of office of the directors of other counties have also expired, including Chen Ren of Fengxian, Huang Mingzhang of Jinshan, Jia Fengyun of Shanghai, Chuan Gongbi of Nanhui, Zhang Shoufeng of Qingpu, and Zhang Zhihe of Chuansha. The county government has sent separate letters to each county to recommend replacements for appointment.

Gunshots in the Dark Night Discovered to Be a Fire Alarm: The military, police, and various agencies in the city suddenly heard several gunshots coming from the southwest last night (22nd) at two o'clock. The garrison immediately deployed troops and stood on the city walls to scout. Zhu Huanbo, the director of the county Public Security Bureau, also sent police to deploy in case of emergency. Later, it was reported that a thatched house belonging to a certain family in Da Zhangjing suddenly caught fire. The thatch and bamboo rafters on the roof had been dried by the intense sun, and once ignited, they crackled loudly.

Re-survey of Disaster-Stricken Cotton Fields: The cotton fields in Tuolin Township have been damaged by hail. There is also damage in the territory of the Second District. The county government commissioned a section member to conduct an on-site inspection. The committee member's reply stated that the disaster-stricken land in Zhangjiabang and Wujiajiu townships in the Second District has been replanted with seeds that have been purchased. The growth of these plants is later than the originally planted ones, and it is difficult to predict the harvest. He then went to Tuolin one, two, three, four and five maps, and found that, due to years of famine, he was unable to purchase seeds for replanting in each area. Most of them were replanted with sweet potatoes and soybeans, which are not as productive as cotton. The losses to rural farmers are particularly dire.

Plotting Prison Escape: The prisoner was sent to the county for questioning: The county prison inmates plotted to escape the night before last but were fortunately discovered by prison official Zhang Zonglie, averting the incident. It was determined that thirty inmates had filed through their shackles in an attempt to escape, all of whom were serious offenders. Prison Official Zhang reported this to the county government for interrogation. It is said that the masterminds were Wang Weishu and others, who had bought and transported files into the prison. It was first discovered by the old inmate Li Shuangxi, who reportedly will be recommended to the High Court for an award. The interrogation of the prisoners has not yet been completed.

Suzhou

The Original Sentence is Upheld in the Case of Plotting to Murder a Stepmother: Cai Yishan, from Changshu Baoben Street, who plotted to murder his stepmother, as well as the coachman Qian Zengzeng, and clansmen Cai Jinshi and Cai Lishi, appealed to the High Court, dissatisfied with the death sentence and life imprisonment handed down by the Changshu County judicial authority. The verdict was announced yesterday (23rd): Cai Yishan and Qian Zengzeng were still sentenced to death, and Cai Jinshi and Cai Lishi were still sentenced to life imprisonment. After the verdict, Cai Yishan and others stated that they were dissatisfied and would appeal to the Supreme Court.

Wuxian County is Assigned to Raise 80,000 *kuan*: County Magistrate Huang Yunshang and Finance Bureau Director Yuan Xiaogu were summoned to the province by Provincial Chairman Ye via telegram. They received instructions from Chairman Ye that the provincial government was acting on the orders of Chairman Jiang to raise 500,000 *kuan*, and Wuxian County was assigned 80,000 *kuan*, using the busy canal transport of the 19th year of the Republic of China as security, and ordered to raise the money immediately. Huang and Yuan returned to Suzhou on the 23rd and will immediately gather gentry, merchants, and other sectors of society to discuss ways to raise the money.

Fengxian

A Major Prison Break Occurred in Fengcheng: Prison breaks have occurred in this county twice in the past year. After the fact, the only punishment was a paper order to arrest the fugitives and a simple dismissal of the warden as a warning. How to handle the aftermath has never been discussed, so it is only natural that this major prison break has occurred again. It is said that the cause of the disaster occurred at around 4:30 PM yesterday (21st), when more than a dozen serious offenders cut through their shackles and rushed out of the gate. The remaining prisoners saw the opportunity and also shouted and cheered from behind. First, they knocked down the guards, seized their rifles, and fired wildly outwards. They then pulled up the wooden fence and used it as a weapon, fleeing for their lives from the east and south gates. The order was immediately disrupted, and everyone panicked. The police from the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau and the Fourth Squad of the police heard the news and sent teams to pursue and suppress the prisoners. However, the distance between the two sides was already half a kilometer, and the terrain was close to the seawall, with roads branching out. It was difficult to both watch out for them and to encircle them. As a result, twelve people were killed and sixteen were captured. The rest scattered and disappeared. Four residents, including the cake seller A Da, were injured by stray bullets. County Magistrate Shen Qingchen personally went to inspect the scene and ordered squad leader Ding Zhiyan to lead a team to search through the night. According to reliable reports, three more people were captured in the Tangjiao area this morning. In total, forty to fifty prisoners escaped.

Xiaotang Cracked Down on Child Carrying Opium: The Xiaotang Public Security Police Station investigated a rural child over ten years old who was surrounded by local bullies on the street yesterday. They immediately went to stop them. The child suddenly took the opportunity to escape. Because his actions were suspicious, they chased him back and searched him. It was found that he had more than twenty bags of Yu Changchuan opium in his arms. It is said that the opium was entrusted to him by relatives. He has now been sent to the headquarters and transferred to the county for interrogation.

The Calligraphy Exhibition is Opening Soon: The County Second Public Education Hall is launching a calligraphy and painting exhibition in Fengcheng to promote art and cultivate individuality. The opening date is set for August 10th to 20th. Collectors from various districts have been sending old and new works for display. In addition to calligraphy and painting, there are also many kinds of stone inscriptions. As of yesterday, more than 2,000 items have been collected. It is expected that there will be a grand occasion at that time.

Wujiang

Refugees from Pingjiang, Hunan Arrive in the City: Three hundred and eighty male, female, old, and young refugees from Pingjiang County, Hunan Province, arrived from Dongting Mountain, Wuxian County, yesterday afternoon and moored near the Sanjiang Bridge outside the east gate. The Chief Inspector of the County Public Security Bureau, Song Tingyuan, led the police to suppress them. The refugees said that it was late and agreed to leave the border the next morning.

A Sequel to the Arrest of Three Bandits in the City: On the afternoon of the 19th, the county's water police team arrested three bandits, including Wang Jianchang, in the city and sent them to the troops for preliminary interrogation. They confessed that the weapons were hidden in Xigang Fuxiang. On the morning of the 20th, the team escorted the three bandits to Xigang to search, but it was said that the bandits had moved the weapons earlier, so they were not seized.

Wuxi

Details of Arrest of Impersonator of Regiment Commander: Outside the South Gate of Wuxi, in areas such as Shangxia Tang and Chang Street, stores are densely packed and quite bustling. Unexpectedly, at 8:30 PM the other night, a young man in a Zhongshan suit came to the First Police Station of Shangpailou to report, briefly stating that a group of Suzhou wounded soldiers were causing trouble and were coming to Wuxi by waterway, urging them to prepare quickly. The young man also went to various merchants in Nanchang Street to report. Finally, he went to the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau and reported to bureau officer Li Linshi, generally as described above, and presented a name card (reading: Zhu Maoquan, Regiment Commander, 31st Regiment, National Revolutionary Army, Beimentangtou, Wuxi, Jiangsu). He then excused himself and went into the city. When he reached the South Gate, he ordered the guards there to close the city gate. The guards did not comply because they had not received a formal order. Soon after, merchants in the Nanli area closed their businesses early and turned off all the streetlights, creating an atmosphere of panic and alarm. At the same time, County Magistrate Sun Zuji, after receiving the news, immediately led detectives to investigate secretly. The Public Security Bureau also instructed various branches inside and outside the city to be on high alert. Chen Zhanru and Chen Pinsan, standing committee members of the County Chamber of Commerce, also went to Nanli to conduct on-site investigations. Unexpectedly, at around 9:00 PM that night, the young man went to the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau outside Guangfu Gate and made the same report. Branch Chief Sun and Inspector Qian questioned him in detail. According to the young man, his name was Zhu Maoquan. He came to Wuxi from Suzhou today and went to the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau to visit a friend named Xu. He also claimed that a Regiment Commander Zhang would come to Wuxi tonight. "My regiment commander is Zhang; he quit and gave the position to me." When asked about the location and structure of the regiment headquarters, he hesitated and appeared flustered. Sun and Qian, believing that the young man Zhu Maoquan was clearly impersonating a military officer and spreading rumors to confuse the public, immediately arrested him and sent him to the Public Security Bureau. Section Chief Qian Yaonian of the Third Section held a court hearing. Zhu Maoquan confessed that he was nineteen years old, lived in Zhu Lane, Beimentangtou Town. Last year, he was in the business of selling water pumps in Wuxi. Recently, he had been staying home idly. A few days ago, after drinking, he went to the Huadong Printing Company to print military rank cards. He falsely reported to the Third Branch that Suzhou wounded soldiers were robbing people, etc. After hearing the confession, Section Chief Qian believed that Zhu Maoquan dared to impersonate a military officer and spread rumors to confuse the public, which was despicable. He immediately prepared a document and sent him to the county government for legal questioning. Yesterday, Committee Member Tang held a court hearing and ordered his detention pending legal proceedings.

The Levying of Sutra Chanting Donations Has Not Stopped: The County Finance Bureau recently received reports from various district sutra chanting donation collection offices stating that when the people in various districts encounter sutra chanting ceremonies, they often use the excuse that the central government has ordered a halt to the collection of sutra chanting donations as reported in the newspapers and delay payment, resulting in a significant reduction in revenue. However, the bureau has not received a provincial order to stop the collection. Yesterday, it issued a notice stating that until a provincial order is received, the old rules must still be followed and they must not wait and see, which would hinder the special education fund.

Crackdown on Armed Robbery of Opium Case: According to recent news, Li Zaiyang, the squad leader of the third team of the second district of the Jiangsu Water Police Team, cracked the case of Qian A'gen and Yao Shunfu, who used weapons to rob thirty-six dan of opium near Wangting. They were immediately sent to the second district, where District Chief Mao Mujun personally questioned them. Qian A'gen confessed that he was thirty-five years old and worked as a boatman. The opium he was transporting was contracted by my old man, Zhu Youlin, and he gave me 200 yuan for the boat fare. Zhu is now working as the chief detective of the second department of the Shanghai-based Water Police Second District. Yao Shunfu confessed that he was thirty-six years old, from Nanqian, Wuxi. Originally, he was a farmer, but now he runs a tea shop on Nanqian Street, also selling machine-made noodles. On the afternoon of May 23rd, Zhu Youlin came to drink tea and offered to sell me opium. I introduced him to Yao A'tu to buy 213 taels of opium. I paid 435 yuan in silver at that time. Later, I learned that Zhu was the chief detective, etc. It is said that in this case, thirty-six dan of opium were seized. Afterwards, Zhu received seventeen dan, Xiao received one dan, Pockmarked Shuangxi (i.e., Old Master Gu) received one dan, someone received four dan, someone received five dan, and the distribution of the other eight dan is unknown. Xiao originally lived with Zhu outside Guangfu Gate on Dongxin Road. Since this case occurred, they moved to another place, so they are quite involved in this case.

Changshu

Xu Bingsong's Regretful Suicide After Killing His Wife: Xu Bingsong of Xixiang Bridge Town, Pucheng District, was a bamboo craftsman. His wife, Cao, had a strained relationship with him. On the tenth of this month, Xu and Cao quarreled. Several days later, neighbors became suspicious when they did not see Cao outside. So, someone went to Xu Bingsong's house to inquire about Cao's whereabouts. The district office also received a report and sent personnel to Xu Bingsong's house for investigation on the afternoon of the 19th. At that time, Bingsong's sister-in-law, Miao, came out to greet them. Bingsong was also at home. He then went to the workshop under the pretext of getting matches and committed suicide with a cleaver in the workshop. When the investigators went to see, Bingsong was already lying in a pool of blood. Only then did they realize that there was more to this case. The district office then ordered the Baozheng to guard Bingsong's body. For the sake of caution, the local Public Security Bureau went to Xu's house for investigation that evening. Under the grass nest behind Cao's bed, they found a pile of mud about five or six inches high, which was quite suspicious. They presented the entire situation to the County Government Public Security Bureau and requested that they send personnel to inspect it immediately. On the morning of the 21st, Investigating Officer Cen, along with Inspector and Doctor Huang Chengxi, rushed to the village. After arriving at Xu's house, according to the statements of Xu Bingsong's brother and Miao, they moved the grass nest and dug away one or two feet of topsoil. Cao's body was there. Both legs had been cut off, and a cloth strip was wrapped around her neck, indicating strangulation. According to Xu Bingsong's brother, the deceased was indeed his sister-in-law, and Xu Bingsong's death was confirmed as suicide. Investigating Officer Cen then ordered the preparation of a coffin for burial.

Provincial Order to Remit 50,000 Yuan: Wu Deyao, Magistrate of Wuyi County, and Liu Hongzhao, Director of the Finance Bureau, were simultaneously summoned to the province by Chairman Ye of the Provincial Government and Director Chen of the Finance Department. Magistrate Wu and Director Liu went to the province on the 21st to meet with Chairman Ye and Director Chen. Chairman Ye instructed the two county and bureau heads to be responsible for raising funds. After repeated discussions, it was decided to raise 50,000 yuan and remit it to the province by the end of the month. It is also heard that a total of eleven county and bureau heads were summoned to the province at the same time.

The First Branch of the Public Security Bureau Implements Prostitution Ban: Tang Renjie, Chief of the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau of Wuyi, received an order to ban prostitution. He stipulated the first step as taking photos for registration and the second step as sending them to the hospital for education and rehabilitation. On the evening of the 21st, they apprehended four local prostitutes, Zhou Xiaomei, Qian Jinfeng, Wu Jinfeng, and Diaojiao Lao San, in various hotels. After Chief Tang reprimanded them on the 22nd, he ordered that photos be taken for registration. One of them, Diaojiao Lao San, claimed to have reformed and was released on bail after providing a guarantor.

Provincial Police Team Kills Bandits and Seizes Weapons in Yudong: The tenth and fifteenth companies of the Provincial Police Team surrounded and suppressed bandits in Xiaochuan Port, Yudong, at 3:00 AM on the 22nd. After a fierce battle until 9:00 AM, more than eighty bandits were killed, and eight submachine guns, six Mauser pistols, and two rifles were seized. A soldier named Zhou Weixin from the Provincial Police Team was injured and has been sent to the affiliated hospital of Nantong Medical College for treatment.

Various Circles Discuss Measures to Protect the Collapsing Riverbank: The collapse of the Nantong riverbank is dangerously severe. On the 22nd, various circles held a meeting at the county government to discuss ways to protect it. The following measures were decided upon: (1) Raise 30,000 yuan to build a setback embankment with stone; (2) Appeal to the province to allocate funds to assist with work relief; (3) Continue to levy land tax to protect the embankment.

Chengxi Sailing Boat Robbed En Route: A Chengxi sailing boat was sailing from Cheng to Xi last night (the 21st) when it was near Erwan, South Gate, when it was suddenly ordered to stop by three or four bandits. After boarding the boat, they searched and robbed it. Because there were very few passengers, the losses were not great. Afterwards, the South Gate Security Corps heard the alarm and went to investigate, but the thieves had already fled far away. Investigation of the Chengxi Northern Section Project: The Chengxi Road Northern Section project has been repeatedly requisitioned, and work has been intermittent. Much of the earthwork for the entire road has not been completed. Since Mao Feng, Director of the Construction Bureau, took over, he intends to expedite the Chengxi Road project as soon as possible. He specially dispatched technicians to survey the entire road. The results of the inspection showed that the total length of the various sections is forty-three li. Very little had been done before, and most of what had been done had been converted back into farmland. The original roadbed is difficult to identify. In the future, the implementation of the project should still start from scratch. As for the culverts, originally planned for forty-seven, eight of them should be changed to small bridges. Recently, farmers have requested changes for transportation reasons. Yesterday, Director Mao presented the inspection situation to the county for reporting to the Construction Department for processing.

Rugao

Jiali Primary School Set on Fire Again by Bandits: Jiali Primary School in Lugang District of this county was set on fire by bandits once last month. Fortunately, the rescue was swift, and no major disaster occurred. Unexpectedly, on the night of the 18th, many bandits came again and set fire to the school, destroying nineteen rooms. All school equipment and books were burned to ashes, with losses amounting to more than 10,000 yuan.

Security Corps Kills a Large Number of Bandits: Zhang, the branch director of the Jiangjiadai bandit gang in Lugang District, Rugao, used 1,000 yuan in silver to incite a mutiny in the Lugang Security Corps and scheduled it for the 16th. Lu Shupingyang, the head of the corps, pretended to agree but secretly informed the local gentry to prepare. On the appointed day, Zhang Guo came with silver, accompanied by three guards. Lu then ordered the execution of Zhang and the other three by firing squad. At the same time, he led a team to the Jiangjiadai area, where he found many unarmed bandits guarding and collecting weapons. They fought bravely and killed as many as sixty-eight bandits. The rest were injured and fled.

Bandits Attack Luzhuang and Are Completely Defeated: At around 4:00 PM on the 16th, a group of over a thousand bandits suddenly surrounded Luzhuang. The provincial and county police teams stationed in the village and the security corps divided up to resist. Just then, Commander Li Changjiang led a team to the village and ordered a vigorous suppression. Soon, the local garrison troops also arrived one after another and joined in the encirclement. After a fierce battle for more than ten hours, the bandits were unable to resist and retreated. More than a hundred bandits were killed on the spot, and two guns were seized. Police officer Wang Jingui and corps member Qin Yuanhai sustained minor injuries but are not in serious condition.

Detailed Report on the Tragedy at the Dade Company in Chenjiagang, Lianshui: After the position of General Manager Ye Shaolan of the Dade Salt Company in Chenjiagang, Lianshui, was vacant, the company authorities promoted the former Deputy General Manager Xu Xinbo to General Manager and promoted Zhu Chunjiang, the captain of the company's security team, to Deputy General Manager. Unexpectedly, Zhu did not meet the public's expectations, and everyone opposed him. All other company employees threatened to resign. Zhu knew that the case was serious and difficult to escape, so he shot himself and died. However, Sun and Cheng had minor injuries and were treated by doctors. Their lives were not in danger. Only Zhu and Xu died on the spot. Yesterday morning (the 19th), the coffins of the two were transported to Pu. Xu's coffin was temporarily placed in the temple. Zhu was from Jiangdu County. It is said that his coffin will be transferred to Yangzhou.

New Look in Front of Ziyun Temple: There is an old square area inside the east and west archways of Ziyun Temple outside the east gate of this port city. Behind the screen wall in front of the gate is the commonly known Yue Long Pond. Recently, Huaiyin has started to operate tour boats for people to hire for sightseeing, and the wharf outside the city has been designated there. Therefore, the monks of the temple voluntarily opened the flower walls on both sides of the screen wall to create two Western-style gates, and paved a road from Flower Street to reach the water's edge, so that tourists could get on and off the tour boats. On one side, they built five thatched halls in the square for people to rest. Furthermore, they organized a vegetarian restaurant called Gongdelin in the temple. As a result, the quiet and deserted ancient temple has taken on a new look.

Department of Finance Approves Delay of Penalties in Various Counties: The collection of land tax offset gold in various counties of Zhejiang Province is divided into busy and less busy seasons. If it is not fully paid three months after the start of each busy season, a fine should be imposed. It is now learned that the magistrates of various counties in the province reported that last year, various places suffered heavy disasters and the people's strength was not enough. If penalties were imposed hastily, the people's burden would become heavier and it would be more difficult to collect taxes. Therefore, they have been requesting the Department of Finance to extend the penalty period by one month to alleviate the people's hardship. The Department of Finance has now investigated the situation in various places and confirmed that there are indeed difficulties. It has replied to the counties, approving the extension of the busy season silver and grain payment.

The other day, she had a secret rendezvous with Gu at the home of Wang Yanchang, a neighbor on the street, and agreed to continue the pleasure at Pingyang Mountain in the evening. A young passenger, about twenty years old, with a thin face and looking like he had lung disease, came to the large third-class cabin. He claimed to be surnamed Jin and was going to Putuo to recuperate. The wheel arrived in Ningbo at 6:00 AM the next morning. The tea servant did not disturb him because he thought he was a guest for Putuo. However, by 9:00 AM, the wheel turned and left Ningbo, about to arrive at Putuo, the passenger had not gotten up. Knocking on the door to investigate, the guest had disappeared. A summer cloth gown and a leather suitcase (containing 26 yuan in silver) and objects such as fountain pens and diaries were left in the room. In the diary, there were the words "Jin He of Jiaxing" and many pessimistic short articles. At 11:15 AM, the wheel's radio station suddenly received a telegram in English from the Wusong radio station, saying that a person named Jin Ziwen wanted to commit suicide by jumping into the sea on your wheel, please stop him. However, the wheel had been unable to prevent it. The telegram did not have the name or address of the sender, so it was impossible to reply at that time. Only all the deceased's belongings were temporarily stored, awaiting relatives to come and claim them.

Letter to the Editor

Letter from the Bengbu Municipal Police Bureau

Esteemed Editor,

Having read the Bengbu dispatch in your esteemed newspaper on the 16th, concerning the matter of police officers agitating for back pay, there are slight discrepancies with the facts. We hereby provide a brief account of the origins of this matter and the financial difficulties faced by our bureau, respectfully requesting its publication to clarify the truth.

The Bengbu Municipal Police Bureau has consistently relied on police tax revenue for its regular expenses and maintenance. Each month, there is a shortfall of approximately six thousand dollars, which was typically subsidized by the provincial government. However, since Shi Yousan's army occupied Bengbu last winter, the bureau chiefs appointed by him, Ying Jingzhai and Huang Guangyuan, successively embezzled funds and fled with Shi. As a result, police salaries have been in arrears for four months.

When our current bureau chief took office in February of this year, he witnessed the hardship of the police officers. Furthermore, due to the devastation caused by Shi's army, all industries were in decline, and police tax revenue sharply decreased, exacerbating the police funding shortage. Consequently, he borrowed over three thousand dollars from gentry and merchants in his private capacity to fully disburse February's police salaries. Staff salaries were discounted and advanced. In March, local authorities provided an additional three thousand three hundred dollars, which barely sufficed to issue police salaries.

Subsequently, our bureau chief, unwilling to further burden the local population, refrained from raising funds locally and directly petitioned the provincial government to investigate and allocate monthly subsidies. Despite written appeals and personal requests to the commissioner, there was no outcome. Therefore, for the months of April, May, and June, police salaries were only distributed on a pro rata basis from police tax revenue, with each person receiving an advance of one or two dollars per month to maintain the status quo.

Recently, our bureau chief, recognizing that prolonged delays would jeopardize the future of police administration, engaged with the chamber of commerce to seek subsidies. Local figures were also understanding of the difficulties and generously agreed to subsidize three thousand dollars to clear the arrears during his tenure, which has been agreed upon. Our bureau chief, further concerned that the current livelihood of the police officers could not be sustained, arranged for an advance of one dollar per person from June's tax revenue as a gesture of goodwill.

Unexpectedly, a few off-duty police officers, not understanding the situation, mistakenly believed that the salary disbursement was limited to this amount, and went to the bureau to question the accountant. At the time, the number of participants was only several dozen. After the situation was explained, the police officers maintained order and there was no disturbance.

Our bureau has since cleared all outstanding medical salaries for April, May, and June, and local order is exceptionally stable. The sections in the report that say, "almost caused a disaster" are likely due to misinformation and a lack of clarity on the true situation. This letter is specifically for correction, and we hope for your kind consideration, with utmost gratitude.

Sincerely,

Secretariat of the Bengbu Municipal Police Bureau, July 20th
