Education News

Important News

Regulations of the Jiangsu Education Department

Service Rules for Principals of Provincial Middle and Primary Schools

The Jiangsu Provincial Government has successively formulated the Organizational Regulations for Jiangsu Provincial Middle Schools and the Regulations on the Appointment, Employment, and Treatment of Middle School Principals, all of which have been published in this newspaper. However, the service rules for principals of middle and primary schools have been lacking. In view of this, the Jiangsu Education Department has, based on educational laws and regulations and careful consideration of local conditions, separately formulated service rules for principals of middle and primary schools. We now publish the relevant details of these rules below:

(1) Service Rules for Principals of Jiangsu Provincial Middle Schools

Article 1: These rules are formulated in accordance with Article 9 of the Regulations on the Appointment, Dismissal, and Treatment of Principals of Jiangsu Provincial Middle Schools.

Article 2: The duties of a principal of a provincial middle school are as follows: (A) Regarding the management of school affairs: 1. Lead faculty and staff in implementing Party ideology and educational laws and regulations. 2. Represent the school externally. 3. Convene school affairs meetings and various committees. 4. Implement resolutions of school affairs meetings and various committees stipulated by laws and regulations. 5. Allocate duties and salaries to faculty and staff. 6. Evaluate teacher performance and determine promotions and demotions. 7. Supervise administrative staff, organize curriculum, create school administrative calendars, and various application forms, and compile statistics on the progress of school affairs. 8. Handle student admissions and withdrawals. 9. Issue certificates of completion, graduation, and transfer. 10. Oversee school-wide discipline. 11. Safeguard school finances and manage school property. 12. Prepare budget estimates and final accounts for submission and review. 13. Plan school facilities and construction projects. 14. Promote school hygiene and student physical and mental health examinations. (B) Regarding research: 1. Implement the teaching order established by the central and provincial departments. 2. Adopt new teaching methods and their implementation steps. 3. Examine social needs as a standard for reforming teaching. 4. Lead faculty and staff in organizing academic research associations. 5. Edit publications and report research experiment results. 6. Organize academic lecture meetings. 7. Instruct on teaching training and methods for handling school affairs. 8. Guide other matters available for research.

Article 3: The principal may not handle the following matters on their own without submitting them to the Education Department for approval: 1. Increasing or decreasing classes. 2. School building construction and special repairs. 3. Use of school and accommodation fees. 4. Disposal of school property. 5. Use of reserve funds within the budget. 6. Joint activities outside the school. 7. Other matters not within the principal's authority.

Article 4: The principal must be at school during office hours, except on holidays, to supervise staff.

Article 5: The principal may not leave their post without applying for leave. If leave exceeds one week, a designated acting officer must be appointed to take responsibility for performing their duties. The acting officer must also be reported to the Education Department for record.

Article 6: These rules shall be promulgated and implemented by the Jiangsu Provincial Education Department and reported to the Ministry of Education and the Provincial Government for record.

(2) Service Rules for Principals of Jiangsu Provincial Middle School Experimental Primary Schools

Article 1: These rules are formulated in accordance with Article 9 of the Provisional Regulations on the Appointment, Dismissal, and Treatment of Principals of Jiangsu Provincial Middle School Experimental Primary Schools.

Article 2: The functions and powers of the principal of an experimental primary school are as follows: (A) Regarding research experiments: 1. Formulate the policies and steps for experimental new education methods. 2. Attend middle school normal course meetings to seek connections between normal schools and primary school teaching. 3. Guide faculty and staff to engage in experimental education. 4. Supervise faculty and staff in organizing research associations for earnest research. (B) Regarding the handling of school affairs: 1. All matters related to the administration of the respective middle school shall be handled under the direction of the middle school principal. 2. Approve the proposals and work of faculty and staff. 3. Represent the school and handle all external negotiations. 4. Convene school affairs meetings and act as chairman. 5. Examine the work performance of faculty and staff as a standard for promotion and demotion. 6. Decide on the tasks and salaries of faculty and staff. 7. Plan the construction of school buildings. 8. Compile the school administrative calendar. 9. Handle matters of student admission and withdrawal. 10. Allocate teaching subjects and teaching time. 11. Coordinate teaching material outlines and teaching books. 12. Issue certificates of completion, graduation, and all honorary certificates to children. 13. Guide the preparation of various forms, registers, and books. 14. Pay attention to the uniformity of school-wide discipline. 15. Pay attention to the development of children's autonomous activities. 16. Improve the school's environment and facilities. 17. Pay attention to maintaining school hygiene. 18. Connect with student families and examine social needs. 19. Prepare budgets and review final accounts. 20. Plan the experimental outline for experimental education. 21. Edit publications and report experimental research results. 22. Handle matters designated by the Education Department. (C) Regarding guiding local education: 1. Each school year, visit local education in each district and county once, and submit the findings to the Education Department for review. 2. When examining education, report on the school's experimental process and results. 3. When examining education, provide systematic and concrete lectures to meet local needs. 4. During normal times, be responsible for correspondence research with local schools and for guidance and responses. 5. Supervise local education instructors to provide circuit guidance to local education within the district. 6. Guide local education research associations to bear the responsibility for improvement. (D) Regarding guiding teacher training: 1. Contact the middle school normal department to organize a teacher training practice guidance committee. 2. Before teacher training, report on the school's situation. 3. During teacher training, provide instruction on teaching, discipline, and methods for handling school affairs, and supervise practice. 4. After teacher training, hold criticism meetings and research meetings, and evaluate merits and demerits, compile statistics on performance, and send them to the normal department. 5. After teacher training graduates, form an introduction department with the main staff of the normal department to introduce service locations.

Article 3: The principal of the experimental primary school should work at the school during office hours every day, except when going to various counties for inspection.

Article 4: The principal of the experimental primary school may concurrently serve as a teacher in the normal department or as an honorary position outside the school, as long as it does not interfere with school affairs.

Article 5: The principal of the experimental primary school may not leave their post without applying for leave. If leave exceeds one week, a designated acting officer must be appointed to take responsibility for performing their duties. The acting officer must also be reported to the Education Department for record. Article 6: These rules shall be promulgated and implemented by the Jiangsu Education Department and reported to the Ministry of Education and the Provincial Government for record.

Measures for Identifying and Prohibiting the Export of Ancient Books

The Ministry of Education drafted instructions on identifying and prohibiting the export of ancient books. Chen Fu, Executive Secretary of the Secretariat, said, "Received your department's letter of the 7th of this month, regarding the Ministry of Finance's request for the approval of a case to ban the export of ancient books, and instructed the ministry to deliberate and respond. Also approved the transfer of the original memorial. After reviewing the various points of the original memorial from the Ministry of Finance, they are indeed essential. In order to facilitate implementation, the Ministry has drafted the 'Instructions for Identifying and Prohibiting the Export of Ancient Books' to facilitate implementation. Enclosing a copy of the instructions, please review, approve, and issue a strict prohibition order, and circulate these instructions for implementation." The original text of the "Instructions for Identifying and Prohibiting the Export of Ancient Books" is as follows: (1) Ancient books prohibited from being exported temporarily include the following types: 1. Thread-bound books or paintings exquisitely printed on woodblocks that meet one of the following conditions: A. Published during the Song, Yuan, or Ming dynasties. B. Various palace editions and fine editions published during the Qing dynasty. C. Editions published more than 50 years ago and whose original printing blocks no longer exist. 2. Yongle Encyclopedia and Siku Quanshu. 3. Archival historical materials. 4. Handwritten manuscripts. 5. Fine-edited versions. (2) Sun Yat-sen's unpublished works and calligraphy are strictly prohibited from being exported. (3) Lithographic, photographic reprints, and seal prints are not subject to the export ban. (4) When identifying the above ancient books, the following procedures should be adopted: 1. For woodblock ancient books, the publication dynasty or year shall prevail. If the dynasty or year is unclear, the year of the preface shall prevail. If the year of the preface is unclear, the years of the author of the preface's life shall prevail. 2. If there are any doubts about the identification of the aforementioned items, the original book must be sent to the Ministry of Education for identification. 3. If there are too many volumes of the ancient books that should be sent, a few volumes may be sampled and sent, or the Ministry of Education may send personnel to identify them.

Rejection of the Christian Church's Request to Establish Religious Studies Courses

Fan Dingjiu and other representatives of the Chinese Christian Church submitted a request to the Ministry of Education for permission to allow church schools at all levels to offer elective religious courses and to hold religious ceremonies in primary schools. After receiving the request, the Ministry of Education rejected it yesterday. The original rejection stated, "Received the request and examined the matters mentioned, there are some misunderstandings. Explanations are provided item by item as follows: (1) 'Using religious doctrines to cultivate life' is a valid point, but it should be based on drawing on the spirit of various religions, such as Buddhism's equality and compassion, and Christianity's universal love and helping others... It should not be limited to one religion, nor should it be merely formal. Establishing a specific course limited to one religion and holding religious ceremonies are formalistic and not what educationally means by cultivation. (2) The restrictions on religion in the regulations for private schools are not limited to one religion. If any religion indoctrinates underage junior high school students or younger with doctrines, making them prejudiced by a certain religion, it is tantamount to depriving them of the freedom to choose a religion in the future, which is truly 'shackling the freedom of thought in life.' (3) Since the association, etc., aims at popularizing education and has no intention of using schools to entice or force students to join the church, then the restriction of 'not allowing religious propaganda' does not violate the association's original intention of running schools. As for the claim that the children of over 200,000 Christians must attend church schools, this is also a sectarian view that should not be maintained for long. (4) Education based on science and social reality is what the state approves. Religion is a kind of illusory and缥缈 imagination, not a theory that can be taught, so it is unnecessary to allow its experimentation. In short, religion is not just one religion. Allowing each to compete in religious propaganda under the name of schools will lead to mutual division and inevitable disputes. In order to prevent problems before they arise, the Ministry has no choice but to impose restrictions. This is not just for the Christian religion. The request to establish elective religious courses in junior high schools and to hold religious ceremonies in primary schools is difficult to approve. It is hoped that you will understand the Ministry's subtle intention of restricting religious propaganda in schools and not argue further about this matter."

Great Dissatisfaction of Students Studying in Japan on Gengzi Indemnity Funds

Due to unbearable oppression and contempt from the Japanese authorities

(Central News Agency) Tokyo Dispatch: Negotiations for the return of China's Gengzi Indemnity funds from Japan have been going on for a long time, but until now, the right to control them has not been successfully obtained and remains in the hands of the Japanese. Among them, more than 300,000 dollars are used to subsidize Chinese students studying in Japan. The order of subsidies is determined according to the qualifications of the schools attended by students in Japan, with different quotas for each province depending on the amount of indemnity borne. The number of people and various situations have been reported in previous news. The Japanese use Gengzi Indemnity funds to subsidize Chinese students in order to buy the favor of Chinese students studying in Japan, to reduce anti-Japanese sentiment, and to avoid accusations of cultural aggression. However, the result is completely the opposite. All students who receive Gengzi Indemnity subsidies hate Japan even more than ordinary students, because the stimulation of oppression is more intense. The right to determine the order of student subsidies rests with the Chinese Student Supervision Office in Japan, and after the office makes a decision, the list is sent to the Eastern Culture Department of the Japanese Ministry of Education, which publishes the subsidy after review. Therefore, the list of students to be subsidized sent by the Supervision Office to the department often encounters problems during the review or is delayed in publication, deliberately creating difficulties. The Chinese Supervision Office can only urge the department and cannot do anything else. For example, female students at Waseda University can be subsidized with Gengzi Indemnity funds in the same order as male students. The Ministry of Education has already issued a clear order to the Supervision Office, and the list has been sent to the department, but due to opposition, it has not yet been published. After the department publishes the list, it notifies the school to which the student to be subsidized belongs. The authorities strictly investigate the ideology, actions, qualifications, and grades of the subsidized students and require them to fill out forms and report back. Only then does the department issue the subsidy, which the subsidized students receive monthly at their school. When receiving the subsidy, the school authorities give a strict lecture, the meaning and content of which are generally the same, with no major differences. The meaning is to absolutely prohibit being pro-Japanese when receiving the subsidy. If there is any anti-Japanese behavior or slight violation of the school's intentions, the subsidy will be immediately cancelled. Under this oppression, Chinese students dare to be angry but dare not speak out. This year, when Senshu University in Japan lectured students receiving subsidies, they said that the Gengzi Indemnity funds were a gift from the Japanese Emperor, and the subsidized students should be grateful to the Emperor. The next season's fees were deducted from the fees received by the students. Such unreasonable words can still come from the mouths of school authorities. The general situation of humiliating Chinese students receiving subsidies can be imagined. (17)

Jiang Menglin Goes to Hangzhou to Handle the Handover of Zhejiang University

Minister of Education Jiang Menglin originally concurrently served as the president of National Zhejiang University. Later, recognizing that he could not divide his time between the duties of the minister and the president of the university, and that it was inappropriate to remotely lead the university for a long time, in order to respect the central government's regulations restricting concurrent positions, he requested the Executive Yuan to forward a request to the National Government to resign from his concurrent position as president of Zhejiang University, and to appoint Shao Peizi as his successor. The National Government has issued an explicit order. Yesterday, Jiang Menglin requested a five-day leave from the Executive Yuan to go to Hangzhou to handle the handover and return to Beijing to devote himself to the work of the ministry.

Overseas Chinese Schools in Korea Increase Benefits

Travel by Car and Ship is at the Same Reduced Price as Japanese and Korean Students

(Central News Agency) Sinuiju Dispatch: There are quite a few overseas Chinese schools in Korea, the earliest of which was established sixteen years ago, with some having as many as two hundred students. However, the Government-General of Korea has not treated overseas Chinese schools the same as Japanese and Korean schools, such as providing special fare reductions for teachers and students on cars and ships. Overseas Chinese schools have never obtained this benefit. Since Consul-General Zhang Weichen arrived last year, he has negotiated with the Korean governor-general for this right. The Overseas Chinese Primary School in Seoul was the first to be granted permission. Now, the Overseas Chinese Primary School in Incheon is requesting the same treatment by citing the precedent, and an agreement has been reached. Therefore, all travel expenses for teachers and students of the school to travel abroad are now treated the same as those of Japanese schools, which is very gratifying and a new record in the history of overseas Chinese.

Opening of the Summer Biology Research Association (Shusheng)

Six-Week Session

Lectures and Sea Collection Held Daily

Xiamen, 17th: Xiamen University and the China Cultural and Educational Foundation are jointly holding a "Summer Biology Research Association" this summer at Xiamen University. The Cultural Foundation is responsible for funding 7,000 yuan, and Xiamen University is responsible for preparation and supplying research institutes and experimental tools. Preparations were completed, and the opening ceremony was held at the Biology Department of Xiamen University at 9:00 am on the 14th of this month. Professors from universities across the country attended, including: Chen Dafu from Sun Yat-sen University in Guangzhou; Hertelmann, Miller, and MacCluer from Lingnan University; Lin Kesheng and Professors Ma and Hou from Peking Union Medical College; Nicholas from Yenching University; Bowling and Hu Jingfu from Yenching University; Lewis and Chen Naxun from Jinling University in Nanjing; Xu Renji and Huang Nong from Jinan University; Zhu Yuanding from St. John's University in Shanghai; Zheng Chengzhang, Chen Xinguo, and Yu Kangrong from Shanghai University; Wu Zhaofa from Soochow University; Mal Xu from Zhijiang University; Liu Chongle from Northeast University in Liaoning; Kellogg from Fukien Christian University; Chen Ziying and Lin Geizhang from Xiamen University; and Futalai from Yinghua College in Gulangyu.

After the opening ceremony, Xiamen University President Dr. Lin Wenqing delivered a welcome speech. Next, Chen Ziying, a member of the Research Association's Preparatory Committee, described the purpose of the Research Association, stating that two biology experts visited Xiamen University last winter and suggested establishing a coastal biology museum to provide biologists with research opportunities. Our President Lin (Wenqing) is also a biologist and highly praised the proposal, and immediately organized a preparatory committee, with me responsible for the experimental aspects of the work. In recent years, Chinese biological sciences have also made significant progress, and many people return from studying in Europe and the United States every year. However, every summer, they go to various coastal biology museums in Europe and the United States for research, while China lacks such opportunities. For a long time, people have proposed building one, but due to various difficulties, it has not been realized. This year's research association is the beginning of the construction of a coastal biology museum. This month, we will see what the interests of the participants are. If there is strong interest, then with everyone working together, the coastal biology museum can be built soon. This is the meaning of this research meeting. The key elements for the establishment of a coastal biology museum are talent and economy, and talent is even more important than economy. You are all domestic biology experts, and with your cooperation, we hope it can become a reality. After the meeting, the work began, and the time was set for six weeks. The procedure is as follows: work will begin on July 14, the first evening lecture will be held at 7:00 pm on the 19th, the first sea collection will be held on the 20th at Nantaiwu, the second evening lecture will be held at 7:00 pm on the 26th, the second sea collection will be held on August 2nd at Gulangyu, a meeting of biology teachers will be held at 7:00 pm on the 9th, a seaside tea party will be held at 6:00 pm on the 15th, the fourth evening lecture will be held at 7:00 pm on the 16th, the third sea collection will be held on the 17th at Jimei and Liuwudian (amphioxus production area), a meeting of the China Coastal Biology Museum will be held at 7:00 pm on the 18th, farewell will be held at 6:00 pm on the 23rd, and the meeting will open on the 24th.

All travel and food expenses for the participating biologists will be provided by the Research Association. This year, the professors will conduct systematic and specialized research on amphioxus, and they will also choose their own research areas.

Funding for Anhui University Confirmed

The funding for Anhui University in the 18th year of the Republic was 730,000 yuan. When the provincial government compiled the budget for the 19th year, it was changed to 260,000 yuan and noted that it would be finalized after the new president took office. Now, after the 120th Standing Committee meeting of the provincial government, it was resolved to change the school's funding for the 19th year to 360,000 yuan for regular expenses and 100,000 yuan for temporary expenses, totaling 460,000 yuan.

Hubei Education Department Changes the Issuance of Foreign Exchange for Government-Funded Students Studying Abroad

Changing the Amount of National Currency to the Amount of Foreign Currency

Provincial Government Order Approved

The Hubei Provincial Education Department stated that in the past, all provinces issued national currency for the travel expenses of government-funded students studying abroad in the East and the West. However, international transportation usually uses gold coins from Eastern and Western countries. At a time when gold prices are soaring, if the travel expenses for studying abroad are still calculated according to the original amount of national currency, they will be reduced by more than one-half in disguise. According to the actual situation, this is far from sufficient. Recently, according to the joint request of Chen Li and other government-funded students who were admitted to study in the East and the West this year, the travel expenses for studying abroad should be changed to the currency of the country of study. After verification, it seems appropriate. Therefore, it is proposed to temporarily change the issuance of travel expenses for studying abroad this time to the currency of the country of study and to determine the amount according to the actual situation. A list is also provided below:

Country of Study Original Travel Expenses (National Currency) Proposed Travel Expenses (Foreign Currency)

Japan 100 yuan (National Currency) 60 yen (Japanese Gold)

UK 800 yuan (National Currency) 50 pounds (British Gold)

Belgium 800 yuan (National Currency) 50 pounds (British Gold)

USA 1000 yuan (National Currency) 500 dollars (US Gold)

A document and a table were submitted to the provincial government for review. After the 43rd provincial government meeting, it was resolved to approve the proposal, but only for this time.

Students of Zhongshan University Go to Beijing to Petition for Funds

Guangzhou National Zhongshan University, due to its existing school buildings being insufficient and severely damaged, urgently requiring repairs, had its request for 200,000 yuan for repair funds approved by the National Government. Presidents Dai and Zhu of the university, in order to plan for the university's long-term development, designated several thousand acres of land in Shipai, Guangzhou, as the permanent site for the university and submitted a request to the National Government for 2,000,000 yuan in new school building construction funds. These two items of expenditure, which had long been approved by the National Government, have not yet been allocated for a long time, resulting in the university's existing school buildings still unable to be repaired. Therefore, the student union of the university elected representatives Li Weiguang, Chen Xiezhong, Pan Jun and three others to go to Beijing to petition the National Government. The representatives arrived in Beijing on the 21st and went to the National Government on the 22nd to request the prior allocation of 200,000 yuan for repairs and personally delivered a petition.

Wuxian Education Bureau Adds Public Education Centers

The Wuxian Education Bureau, considering public education centers to be beneficial tools for popularizing education, has launched a pilot program of four centers, appointing four directors to prepare for them: Lu Enrong for the fifth public education center (Weiting), Huang Wenying for the sixth (Hengjing), Xie Zhongcui for the seventh (Jiaozhi), and Wei Yingsun for the eighth (Zhouzhuang). The start-up cost for each center is 400 yuan, and the recurring cost is 150 yuan per month. Once they are successfully established, the monthly funding will be increased to 350 yuan, equal to that of the existing first, second, third, and fourth public education centers, it is said.

The Problem of the Principal of the Fudan University Experimental High School

A Letter from the Alumni Association to Principal Li

The Fudan Alumni Association is in dispute over the replacement of the principal of the alma mater's Experimental High School. The following is the letter from the association to Principal Li and the members of the Experimental High School:

Dear Principal, Greetings. Today, the alumni association held a joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees to discuss the dispute over the principal of the Experimental High School. We carefully reviewed the minutes of the meeting of the faculty and staff of the Experimental High School on June 20, the declaration of Kuai Shixun and others, and the articles of agreement signed by you and the representatives of the Experimental High School in May of the 18th year of the Republic. We know that you designated one of the three candidates elected by the faculty and staff as the principal in accordance with Article 3 of the agreement, which is perfectly legal. We also know that the person who led the declaration was the recorder of the meeting. After repeatedly comparing the declaration and the minutes of the meeting, we found that the declaration only mentioned Articles 1 and 2, while Articles 3 and 4, which stipulate that the principal appoints the principal and hires and fires faculty and staff, were not mentioned at all. Therefore, we suspect that the statements you made as recorded in the minutes of the meeting may not be entirely truthful. They went to great lengths to first seize the principal's decision-making power, and then to bind Principal Chen's will, ensuring that the person they supported would be elected immediately before they could rest assured. They echoed each other, displaying their ability to manipulate the situation. Although we were not present, the situation of being surrounded at the time is vividly depicted on paper. We firmly believe that you will be able to uphold the agreement, exercise your authority, and not be swayed by slander, so as to forever preserve the honor of Fudan University and comfort the hopes of all the alumni. We hope so, we hope so. With respectful greetings, The Executive and Supervisory Committees of the Fudan University Alumni Association

The Compilation of Four-Corner Indexing

The Second Class of the Training Institute Started Yesterday

Japan-Finland Track and Field Competition

A Friendship Match Before the International University Games

(Finnish Dispatch) After Japan's victory in the 9th Far Eastern Games, the strength of its track and field athletes was suddenly shocked by the world. The 12 new Far Eastern records created were close to world records. Therefore, the Japanese jumped to fight with national players. The 4th International University Games will be held in Germany next month. The Japanese athletes who went to the meeting left on the 18th of last month, passing through Siberia and arriving in Finland on the 15th of this month. In order to entertain the Japanese athletes, the country held a track and field competition on the 16th and 17th.

Chen Yanlu held a track and field competition in the area. Finland's sports have long been known to the world and hold many world records. Japan was not its enemy in the past, but now in the two-nation confrontation, Japan has won many positions. This is a good result for the first battle of its European players. Establishment Meeting of the Shanghai Martial Arts Society

The Shanghai Martial Arts Society held its founding meeting at 7:30 p.m. on July 22nd at the Moxi Stone Printing Workers' Union in Yongfuli, Yongxing Road, Zhabei. More than 40 initiators and members attended. Chen Songchun, representative of the Municipal Education Bureau; Zhang Yunqing, representative of the Municipal Civilian Training Association; Li Guohua, representative of the Sixth District Party Headquarters; Liang Guozhang, representative of the Fourth District Party Headquarters attended. The chairman reported on the preparations and the recent approval of the Municipal Civilian Training Association and the registration procedures with the Municipal Education Bureau, as well as the future development direction of the association. Representatives from higher authorities then delivered speeches, elaborating on the significance of promoting martial arts and encouraging the association to persevere so that its work would develop day by day. Subsequently, elections were held. As a result, Lu Ganhua, Li Guohua, Li Yaozhang, Li Nong, and Zhang Jianmin were elected as executive committee members, Liu Junyan and Liu Chengyong were elected as alternate executive committee members, Hu Desheng was elected as supervisor, and Wu Caifa was elected as alternate supervisor. They were immediately sworn in and took office. After the meeting, the first executive committee meeting was held to determine the responsibilities. The meeting ended at 11 o'clock, it is said.

Shanghai Friends Basketball Team Wins the Game

The Shanghai Friends basketball team is quite fierce. It defeated the strong Western Children's Public School in its first battle. Now, taking advantage of the summer vacation, it has initiated an away game. A meeting was held at the Xueyu Sports Association, and as a result, it was decided to go to Suzhou, with eight players. They will depart on the morning of the 24th and return to Shanghai on the morning of the 26th. Yesterday, in preparation, they specially invited the well-known Qiangnan basketball team to compete. As a result, they won by a large margin of 35 to 15. The players are listed below: (Coach) Yang Jingquan, (Captain) Wu Shiming, (Vice Captain) Xi Shaozheng, (Players) Zhang Zhenda, Wang Guoliang, Zhang Huipu, Chen Aoyin, Zhang Zhenou.

Free Talk

A Word of Wisdom by Hai Ke

Happiness comes from hard work. Misfortune arises from ease and comfort.

The ancients considered it a rare tale that one's eyes may behold courtesans, but the heart holds none.

After reaching the boiling point, love easily unites, but also easily breaks.

If there is no concept of shame between men and women, anything can be done.

If the methods and spirit of seeking love are turned to seeking all careers, success and satisfaction can be easily achieved.

Other things can be done by proxy, but only the work of love must be done in person in everything.

No matter how intimate the friend, there are many heroic acts of commerce and money, but very few large gifts of loved ones.

Eggs must have cracks for flies to swarm. Countries must first be in chaos for foreign insults to follow.

The gun of a military man is sometimes no match for the pen of a scholar. The pen of a scholar is sometimes no match for the money of a rich man.

A Summer Chat in Luanjiang by Liu Huo'an

Twelve Fort used to be called Luanjiang, under the jurisdiction of Yizheng County. It is located on the north bank of the Yangtze River, with beautiful scenery and a clear breeze. The mountain scenery across the river is excellent.

Occasionally coming here to escape the summer heat, idly overlooking the river and the sky, although the river air is connected to the city in the morning, it only exists in fantasy. But the setting sun flickers, watching the sand gulls and sails, and the moon surges in the river, sending a clear breeze. The hardworking travelers have forgotten their worries.

Yizheng is the ancient Zhenzhou. In the early Qing Dynasty, there was a bamboo branch poem by Suiyuan that said, "The water passing through Yangzhou becomes clear, and the salt boats are clustered with poles in the bright evening glow. The sound of the river gradually fades, and the sound of the market is near. A small city is prosperous." The scenery of that year can be imagined.

The arts and literature of Yizheng, such as Liu Yong's "Xiao Feng Can Yue" and Bi Yihong's "Human Hell," are all famous works that will last for thousands of years. It cannot be said that it is not the help of the landscape.

After the Taiping Army, salt merchants moved to the fort. Therefore, the fort has the Yangtze Stack as the salt administration agency. When the famous official Kuai Guangdian was in charge of the stack in the late Qing Dynasty, Zhang Zhidong once came and left a couplet for Kuai: "Accumulated snow in spring, flying frost and dew. Washing soldiers on the island, brushing horses in Jiangzhou." The writing is excellent.

The Jiangxi Guild Hall of the fort is the hometown association of salt boats. I have been back and forth for thirty years, and my feelings for my hometown are deep. I once rashly drafted a couplet for the hall: "The marshland blocks the wind and waves. We are happy to help each other through difficulties. Always make salt and plums harmonize the cauldron. The mind embraces the lakes and seas. I hope we can look forward to the future and transform the drifting water into a family home." The salt boats are divided into eighteen gangs, not just one province. Therefore, the second line is like this.

Guazhou is connected to the fort. When I was a child, I studied in the state. I remember a poem I wrote when I passed through again after two years: "The smoke willows used to lie across the 京口岸, and the waves new shake the tavern." There is no lack of emotion about the vicissitudes of life, which is related to my own life.

Teacher Wang Shaorong died in the state. I wrote a eulogy: "The scholar's heart is eternal, feeling deeply knowing himself. The Yangtze River is one river of water, tears sharing sadness." Tears and ink flow together, is it not the true meaning? (But return)

In Memory of Mr. Sheng Shengchuan by Wu Tingchen

Mr. Sheng Shengchuan, personal name Bingwei, was from Zhenhai County, Zhejiang Province. He was from a distinguished family and passed the imperial examinations early. He successively served as the education commissioner of Sichuan and Jiangxi provinces. After retiring, he advocated public welfare and encouraged younger generations. He had many students, and his descendants were thriving. He was truly a remnant of the former dynasty and a man of the Republic of China. The Sheng family and my family have been friends for generations. Mr. Sheng was also a classmate and close friend of my late father, Hu Qinggong. I have repeatedly thought of visiting the elder, but I often failed because of my work at the newspaper and sleeping late. Last winter, at the funeral of my brother-in-law, Wang Haifan, I also went to mourn. Mr. Sheng happened to be present. I asked my friend Sheng Lansheng to introduce me. After paying my respects, I received much teaching. This spring, I met him again at the home of my brother He Caitang. The next day, I sent a card to visit him, but Mr. Sheng was out on official business. I thought there would be a chance to see him soon, but unexpectedly, Mr. Sheng returned to the Dao Mountain this summer. His dignified appearance is still before my eyes, but his elegant transformation can only be kept in my heart forever. The eulogy is as follows:

Remembering that Mr. and my late father were classmates, they were old friends.

Kneeling Wine by Hui Ling

Mr. Gan Bisheng, styled Bigong, was a famous scholar from Lingnan. He was addicted to chanting poetry and good at drinking. He once poured a full cup of wine at the Liaoshe Poetry Gathering and offered it to the guests, kneeling on the ground to encourage them to drink. Some of the members who could not hold their liquor were all drunk. On the spot, they used "kneeling wine" as the theme and each recited two quatrains. Bigong's poem said, "Why not drink ten cups at once? Pour three more buckets to help the madness. It has always been difficult to bend this knee, not to worship Fenyang, but to worship Ruyang." The demeanor of a famous scholar, letting his heart go freely, is also a good story in the literary world.

Yue descended from the gods, admiring the honored one together. My father's friend followed him from a young age, but never entered the gate to see the beauty and wealth.

Fortunately, you allowed my friend to speak his mind. Since last winter, the Dou Mountain has been in sight, and we have repeatedly received instruction. Why did the wise man wither so suddenly? The fall of the Liangmu is mourned.

The Grand Situation of the National Goods Department Store by Xinsheng

Since the opening of the National Goods Department Store on Nanjing Road last Saturday, the atmosphere has been very good. From 9 a.m. to 10 p.m., buyers have flocked to the store, and each counter has been too busy to handle them all. Because the products are sold directly by the factories, they are priced at wholesale prices. Therefore, they are often more than half the price of imported goods. Most buyers are satisfied. All household necessities, as well as all clothing, food, and utensils, can be found in the store. From this, it can be seen that Chinese people do not need to buy imported goods, and the low price and beauty of Chinese products are actually better than any foreign goods. The decoration of the storefronts is all different and vying for novelty, which is dazzling. The Invincible Brand Department Store is located in a remote corner on the left side of the hall. Its front is obscured by the huge curtain of the Dahua Iron Factory, and the roads on the left and right are also covered by the over-the-street signs of other companies. It should not be visible to the public. However, because of its novel layout, using electric light butterflies to reflect the light through overlapping glass mirrors, it can attract people's attention. Therefore, its business is particularly prosperous. The number of invoices used every day is probably the highest in the company. The reporter has two feelings about this. (1) It is not that Chinese people do not like to use Chinese goods. The phenomenon of the National Goods Department Store is enough to see the psychology of the Chinese people. (2) Sincere and Wing On have also been established for many years. Will the National Goods Department Store necessarily be a flash in the pan? Then, starting from this, to achieve great success, we should wait and see.

The Bai Ying Incident and the Romantic Woman Shao Xie

The Bai Ying incident has become the central topic of discussion in Shanghai society recently. Judging by reason, Bai is indeed a pitiful young woman, and it is the evil environment of society that drives her to this. According to a friend, last summer, when Bai was studying at Fudan University, she often went to Room 39 of the male dormitory to chat. She spoke without restraint and did not act like an ordinary young woman. Bai said, "Men are slaves to women," which is extremely insightful. Later, Bai entered the dance hall and once told her former classmate about her life, saying, "I am now a dancer and can earn three or four hundred yuan a month. In today's society, those who are forced to live in hardship are everywhere. I can also be satisfied." Her meaning was full of emotion. Who would have thought that after a year, it would eventually lead to today's change? Some say that Ms. Bai has a very deep intellect, but she cannot make good use of her emotions, and her actions are romantic, leading to bad consequences.

In general, romantic habits are not necessarily innate, but must be created by the environment. Bai Ying is a good example. A month ago, Ms. Xuan Jinglin produced a film called "Romantic Woman" for the Star Film Company. Although the narrative is not the same as Bai Ying's experience, the depiction of the life of a romantic woman is similar to the Bai Ying incident in all aspects of schools, dance halls, and society. The film tells the story of a young woman who is driven by the environment to fall. The plot is very tortuous, and the background is Shanghai society, with all kinds of monsters and strange things. The film is intended to shock the world. When it is released in the future, those who care about the Bai Ying incident can go and watch it to compare and verify it. They will suddenly realize the evil of society and the difficulty of women to be independent.

The Use of Old Newspapers by Lü Bing

If old newspapers can be accumulated completely, they can be sorted and bound for reference. However, people in society, once

Miscellaneous Records of Gatherings (1)

"Bi Hui" is the name we give to PEN in Chinese translation. PEN is an association of writers initiated in London in 1921 by Mrs. DAWSON SCOTI. But in these few years, it has expanded into an international writers' association. Currently, there are thirty-three participating countries. More than forty cities have established branches, from Oslo to Rome, New York to San Francisco, London to Riga and Helsinki, from Montreal to Buenos Aires, from Geneva to South Africa. Now, with the addition of China, the location of this PEN association has spread across the globe like a spider web. The writers included are poets, playwrights, editors, essayists, and novelists. Broadly speaking, anyone who uses writing as a profession and has achieved a considerable position is eligible to be elected to the association.

The original intention of this association was to provide an opportunity for literary writers in and visiting London to gather and socialize. Its only activity was a monthly dinner. But soon it discovered that there were more things to do than just that. Although it was initially declared that it would not involve politics or any propaganda, this principle is still adhered to today. Its first achievement in Europe was to break down international political boundaries. Before the aftermath of the European war had subsided, German and Austrian writers had already met with writers from the Allied countries through the mediation of PEN. The most significant benefit for a PEN member is that a writer who becomes a member of one branch simultaneously acquires membership of branches all over the world. Therefore, they can enjoy various conveniences when traveling abroad and can get to know literary writers in other countries through the introduction and mediation of various branches.

But PEN also has its greater tasks and greater purposes. Several important resolutions were passed at the annual meeting held in Beijing. 1. Although the origin of literature varies by country, literature itself knows no national boundaries. International or political disputes are inevitable, but literary works should continue to circulate freely between countries.

2. Under any circumstances, especially during wartime, artistic works, being the common property of mankind, should not be subject to destruction by political or national passions.

3. PEN members should use their influence to achieve mutual understanding and respect between nations.

Browsing, often discarding them. Much waste can be utilized; why not old newspapers? Therefore, I offer several points to substantiate this discussion.

Ordinary households often bundle and sell their read newspapers, and the small amount earned per pound is a minor supplement. These newspapers are then resold by vendors to various stalls, where they are used to wrap candies and peanuts, saving costs and providing convenience. This is certainly one way of utilizing them.

When drying clothes in the summer and storing them, if old newspapers are used as lining, it can prevent moths from eating them. Its effectiveness is even greater than that of camphor. This is because the ink used to print on newspapers retains its smell, which is enough to make moths disappear.

Utensils stained by soot and bowls and dishes covered in grease are difficult to wash. Simply wipe them with old newspapers, and they can become clean immediately. After emptying a garbage can, burn some old newspapers inside to keep the can dry and prevent grease from sticking to the walls. This achieves two benefits in one go.

The mattress on an iron bed often develops vertical and horizontal rust stains on its underside due to being pressed upon during sleep. It is difficult to remove these stains. Therefore, several sheets of old newspaper should be laid flat as a barrier to maintain cleanliness and prevent rust.

European Travel Correspondence (63) by Liu Haisu

The French Autumn Salon

(4) A Bird's-Eye View of the 1929 Works (1)

The notice for the Autumn Salon has arrived. It was addressed to MONSIEUR BAI. It was exactly 3:30 PM on October 20th, just as I returned from the Louvre.

Sir,

Your work has been selected. Please come to the venue at 3:00 PM on October 30th to arrange your work. Attached are two invitation tickets and one long-term ticket.

Chairman Xia Deng

This was printed in French on white paper. After we sent the work at the end of September, we didn't have much hope. We had already dismissed the matter. Now, to be selected, it was beyond my expectations.

The afternoon of October 30th was a clear day. We came out of the Louvre, passed through the Tuileries Garden, the Place de la Concorde, and between the Champs-Élysées and the banks of the Seine. Before me stood a magnificent and towering building. When I first arrived in Paris, every time I saw it, I was always amazed. This is a famous historical building in France called the Grand Palais. Above dozens of stone steps, huge sculptures stood side by side, creating a solemn and simple atmosphere that commands respect. This is the entrance to the Autumn Salon.

The Grand Palais is also the old French royal palace. Since 1673, various salons of different eras have been held here. It is a place for people from all countries to appreciate art. The great masters of art from the 18th century onwards in Europe have probably all come here and displayed their works. This alone is enough for us to imagine the glorious history of such a magnificent building. Entering the palace, although crowded, it was very solemn and emitted a deep and rich atmosphere. We bought a "catalog" to follow the map and look at the works one by one. Before I came to the country, I roughly knew the outline of the Autumn Salon. This was the first time I personally saw the Autumn Salon. We first looked at the paintings, going upstairs from the west side. In a larger room at the top of the escalator, we immediately saw a portrait by LATIRON. Four black men were sitting and lying on the beach, talking. The ink-black skin contrasted with the yellow sand and the azure sea. It was a clever and keen stimulus, a kind of lush and beautiful feeling. A morning scene of Notre Dame de Paris. Another nude figure, as white as snow, with lips painted red. This was a Japanese work. Over there, three or four paintings of the lives of Africans were hung. The skin like Coca-Cola, matched with the shady green of the trees, was another kind of lush flavor. Now Matisse has also made a pilgrimage to Tahiti in Fiji. He is looking for the fragrance of Coca-Cola-colored flesh, or the oily green banana trees, and the bright yellow sand. He wanted to discover the true nature of culture and open up new paths in art in a completely barbaric land. I think his future works will definitely have a more strange and vigorous development in color. The first person to paint black people was Monet in his "Olympia." But the most courageous and soulful person who specialized in painting black people and opened up a new artistic sense was Gauguin. Gauguin was indeed vilified for his love of black people. He eventually died on a savage island. Now there are many painters who like to paint black people in Tahiti. This lush flavor has become so common that modern people have become accustomed to it and can no longer produce any different kind of stimulation.

Commercial News

Financial and Gold Markets Increasingly Weak

Fell Another Four Taels Yesterday

Breaking the Ninety-Tael Barrier

Impact of Japanese Political Turmoil

Sluggish Trend and Weary Market Conditions Yesterday, the gold price continued its downward trend. The morning market was relatively stable, but the afternoon market was particularly weak. However, there were no significant fluctuations, only rises and falls of one or two taels. The trend was sluggish, and sentiment was weak. Throughout the day, there was a difference of about seven taels. There were no drastic changes in foreign exchange rates, and quotations remained unchanged. Selling pressure remained strong in the market, with firms such as Da De Cheng and Yuan Sheng selling. Zhi Feng Yong, Yuan Cheng Yong, Shun Li, and Yuan Mao Yong traded intermittently. The buying side was mainly retail customers. The morning market was mediocre, with a slight rise in the silver market, hinting at a potential upward trend around ninety-two or ninety-three taels. In the afternoon, Yuan Cheng Yong, Yuan Mao Yong, Tai Kang Run, and Cheng Feng Yong all sold, while Zhi Feng Yong and Yu Xing Yong bought slightly. The market was quite weak, mainly due to the turmoil in Japanese domestic politics and the reduction of military spending, which triggered general fear and caused prices to plummet by four or five taels, abruptly breaking the five hundred and ninety-tael barrier. However, the gold market unexpectedly turned weak due to the closure of the foreign exchange market on Wednesday. Yesterday, the silver market rose by one-sixteenth, and the U.S. silver price rose by one-eighth.

The Morning Market Was Mediocre, and the Decline Was Slow. The opening price for September was five hundred and ninety-four taels and six mace, an increase of six mace. Subsequently, there were fluctuations of one or two taels, with Yuan Cheng selling and Yuan Cheng Yong buying. When the first order was announced, the quotation remained unchanged at around ninety-four taels. The domestic market was stable, and the wheat firm offered U.S. dollars for August at thirty-seven yuan and bought shillings at six pence two-five, causing the price to rise to ninety-four taels and seven mace. Then, it went downstream due to sales by MacGregor, English gold for October at three seventy-five, September at three one two five, and also by Yuan Cheng and arbitrageurs. After 10 o'clock, it was ninety-one taels and seven mace. Subsequently, there was a slight improvement, and buyers were constantly on the floor, pushing the price up two taels to ninety-three taels and a half at 11:15. Mitsui absorbed October shillings at six pence four three seven five, slightly less than a few cents. Arbitrageurs sold, while Wan Xing and Shun Li bought, resulting in fluctuations of four or five cents. The market closed at noon at ninety-two taels and nine mace, with the revealed price still calculated at six hundred and fifty-two taels and two mace, a small difference of fifty-seven or fifty-eight taels. The noon close was between sixty taels.

Afternoon Close at Ninety Taels. The market opened in the afternoon at ninety-one taels and seven mace, then at one tael and four mace. Sellers were active, and the price was subsequently raised by about two taels to ninety-two taels and four or five mace. It was heard that a small amount of Indian remittances was sold. After that, selling pressure increased, with Heng Xing, Yuan Cheng Yong, and Da De Cheng all competing to sell, causing a drop of three taels to eighty-nine taels after 2:30, breaking the ninety-tael barrier. This was due to weak sentiment and negative atmosphere. After a while, retail customers bought, adding one tael. After 3 o'clock, it was ninety taels and zero two three mace. Sales by Dalian Gang and merchandise caused a sudden drop of more than two taels, and the market was quite weak. At 3:45, it suddenly fell to eighty-seven taels and eight mace. After 4 o'clock, it suddenly jumped up by more than two taels to ninety taels and zero three mace, while Heng Xing's buying and selling were uncertain for unknown reasons. The market closed at 4:30 at ninety taels, a decrease of four taels compared to the previous day. The highest price during the day was ninety-four taels and seven mace, and the lowest was eighty-seven taels and eight mace, a difference of six taels and nine mace. Therefore, there were dual closing prices for the morning and afternoon. The morning price for August was ninety-two taels, and for September, ninety-three taels. The afternoon price was eighty-seven taels to eighty-eight taels. July was already settled, so it was not included. The makeup water was ninety-two taels in the morning and eighty-seven taels in the afternoon. The price of merchandise was four taels and four mace in the morning, two taels and six mace at noon, one tael and six mace in the afternoon, and the closing price was ninety taels.

Selling Pressure Was Strong in the Market. Trading by various firms included Yuan Xing Yong, Yuan Mao, Heng Xing, and Shen Yu all buying. Shun Li, Yuan Cheng Yong, Zhi Feng Yong, Yuan Mao Yong, Jin Da Yong, Yu Da, etc., traded intermittently. Da De Cheng, Yuan Cheng, Yong Cheng Chang, Fu Chang, Sen Chang Yong, and arbitrageurs all sold. In the afternoon, Zhi Feng Yong, Yu Xing Yong, and Fu Yu bought. Da Kang Run, Da De Cheng, Yuan Cheng Yong, Yuan Mao Yong, and Cheng Feng Yong all sold. Heng Xing, Shun Li, Wan Xing, etc., bought and sold occasionally. Dalian Gang bought a total of more than 700 bars and sold more than 600 bars, with no large transactions due to disagreements among arbitrageurs. Guang Gang bought slightly in the morning and traded uncertainly in the afternoon.

Overview of Cotton Crops in Hubei

Best Growth Around Laohekou

Regarding the situation of new cotton in Hubei this year, it is reported that the sowing season this year had more rainfall, about three weeks later than in previous years. The growth situation is as follows: (1) Around Laohekou (Laohekou, Xinye, Zaoyang, Fancheng, Guangshui, etc.), the cotton seedlings had sufficient rainfall, developed well, and the early-planted ones were already over a foot tall. The area suffered less from banditry, and cultivation progressed smoothly. The first weeding work has been completed, and it is predicted that the cotton harvest here is most promising. (2) In the middle reaches of the Han River, such as Shayang, Qianjiang, and Tianmen, there was excessive rainfall, and cultivation was delayed due to banditry. The first weeding has not been completed in half the area, resulting in abundant weeds and poor cotton seedling development. (3) In the Shashi area, there was also excessive rainfall, and part of Jianli was flooded. Furthermore, due to banditry, cultivation was difficult to start, and the cotton seedlings developed slowly, only four or five inches long. The prediction is pessimistic. (4) Along the Pinghan Railway, such as Sancha Bu, Xiaogan, and Yunmeng, development was also slow due to delayed sowing, but the rainfall was moderate, and the situation was quite good. (5) In Caidian Jiaxiang and other places, there was too much rainfall, affecting cultivation, and the development of cotton seedlings was also poor.

Grain: Northern Japonica Rice Continues to Fall, New Japonica Rice Remains Stable

Yesterday, few inland boats arrived at Zhabei, about ten or so. However, the sluggish sales were rare. A small number of northern top-grade japonica rice were still inquired about, but secondary grades were ignored, and the downward trend became more severe, falling a further four jiao compared to the previous day. In total, ordinary japonica rice has fallen by one yuan and three or four jiao within three days, reflecting the sharp drop in inland production prices and active shipments to Shanghai. Since the launch of Dongxin rice in this port, market sentiment has softened significantly, and rice mills are also selling off large quantities of rice in stock. Foreign rice is also falling sharply, creating today's trend, which is a reaction to the large price increase. The volume of Dongxin rice is not strong, remaining only over a hundred dan, so the market remains stable, still at 21 yuan. The situation for Yangxian and Duxian rice remains weak. Observers here believe that goods at 17.5 yuan can be considered ordinary high-quality goods, so the price has dropped significantly. In the afternoon, according to the association's news, foreign rice had shown a firming trend, so the market felt slightly stable. There is very little Xian rice here, with no transactions. Baiyuan high-grade rice is stable, while secondary grades are weak, and sales are not very good, causing the overall market to be sluggish. Trading was very dull here all day, due to the lack of development in the Hujiao market.

The total number of boats arriving at the river docks in Shanghai South was about ten. The market sales in this street are the same as in Zhabei, extremely sluggish. Machine-milled rice, such as special top-quality goods, remains stable, but if goods are slightly below standard, the price cuts are too large, so the market price is another two jiao lower than the previous day's market. The market situation can be described as deteriorating. A small amount of Dongxin rice has been seen, and the sales path is still acceptable, with the price still at 21 yuan. Thin rice boats have been seen arriving, but the sales market is not strong. Stores only selectively purchase high-quality rice, while consumption at meals is even more sluggish. Top-quality goods opened between 20 yuan and 5 or 6 jiao. The situation for Yangdu and Jian rice continues to be weak. Large quantities will be arriving soon, so the future trend is feared to be even weaker. General goods sales are not good, and inventory is gradually increasing, causing the market to soften and trading to be light. The price is down a small amount.

Local News

Jianghai Customs Prohibits the Northern Transport of Rice and Grain

Large Quantities of Rice Are Blocked in Shanghai

Weihai, Yantai, and Tianjin Are All Not Allowed to Be Shipped To

Since the closure of the Tianjin Customs, difficulties have arisen in North-South maritime transport. After requests from various merchants, Tianjin Customs has allowed foreign ships to pay a security deposit, and Chinese ships to submit tax bills as a measure of accommodation. Goods to be transported north can then be inspected and unloaded. However, this year, various parts of our country are suffering from famine, especially North China. Since the outbreak of military operations, the food required by the North has always relied entirely on transport from the South. As a result, a problem has arisen. Recently, because the North has come to Shanghai to purchase and transport large quantities of rice and grain, the Shanghai Jianghai Customs has issued an order prohibiting exports. The details of this matter are recorded separately below.

Purchasing Rice to Be Shipped to Tianjin: The Tianjin area has always needed food supplies, which are entirely purchased from Shanghai. The main item is flour, most of which is undertaken by various flour mills in Shanghai, and transported by sea. This year, a considerable amount of American wheat flour was also shipped during the spring. Recently, since the order prohibiting the export of flour was issued, the Tianjin side has faced a major panic regarding the food supply for the people, due to the reduction in flour coming from the South. About ten days ago, Tianjin officials were dispatched to Shanghai to purchase large quantities of foreign rice. Whether it was Rangoon rice or Annamese rice, all were needed. It is heard that a large quantity has already been purchased. The first batch had already been entrusted to a British merchant ship to be shipped first in several thousand bags, directly to Tianjin for unloading. However, many of the remaining bags are awaiting shipment. The Jianghai Customs' prohibition order has been issued, and they are not allowed to be exported.

Negotiations for Shipment to Tianjin: It is reported that the first batch, which had already been purchased, consisted of tens of thousands of bags. Last week, the person in charge was entrusted to first contact the Chinese Merchant Steam Navigation Company to request that it provide ships for transportation. When the Chinese ships were on vacation, the request to carry the goods was refused. The shipment was then switched to North Sea liners of British and Japanese foreign merchants in this port. Each ship carried 4,000 bags northward at a time, with the unloading location being Tianjin. The foreign merchant ships had already received the goods and were scheduled to report the export after the 20th. They are now being blocked by the Customs.

Prohibition of Reporting Shipment: A certain British ship, which was carrying 4,000 bags of rice and grain, reported to Jianghai Customs that it was exporting the rice to be unloaded in Tianjin. The Customs, having received the order prohibiting the transport of rice to Tianjin, refused to allow the export and immediately returned the customs declaration. The British ship, having promised the customer that it could load the goods beforehand and the business was also large, returned to the Customs and requested to change the unloading destination to Yantai, in order to avoid the prohibition. The ship then reported the shipment again, but was again rejected by the Customs, which stated that Yantai was also within the prohibited transport area and that it was not convenient to change. In the end, the owner of the goods had to ship the rice no matter what, and was willing to have more complicated procedures and pay more for transshipment, but it had to be transported. After consulting with the shipping company, a Westerner from the company personally went to the Customs to request that the port of unloading be changed again for this exported rice, and to be loaded to Weihaiwei for unloading. Weihaiwei is a British leased territory, so it should not be subject to the prohibition. However, under negotiation, it was still not possible to accommodate the request. The Customs still did not allow the export, and the rice that had already been loaded on the ship had to be brought back to the dock.

Transshipment News: According to continued news obtained yesterday, because Weihai, Yantai, and Tianjin cannot be landed in, the owner of the goods is still trying to proceed. It is heard that they have contacted a Japanese shipping company to transport the rice directly from Shanghai to Dalian Bay for unloading, and then transfer it to the Tianjin-Dalian liner, paying an additional freight charge. Whether it can be shipped out is still unknown.

The Consular Body Replies to the Foreign Ministry Regarding the Sale of the Concession Telephone Company

Strong Language

The "North China Daily News" reports that regarding the sale of the Shanghai Chinese-Foreign Telephone Company, the Consular Body has replied to the Foreign Ministry with tactful but firm language. It states that the sale of the company, according to the British Companies Act, has been formally established, and the Shanghai Municipal Council's granting of concession rights to the International Telephone and Telegraph Corporation has also been handled according to proper procedures. In addition, it expresses that the existence of this concession right will not hinder future discussions on the status of the concession.

Pan Gongzhan Discusses the French Concession Water and Electricity Workers' Strike

The Municipal Government Is Conducting Informal Negotiations

The Board of Directors of the Factory Has a Very Strong Attitude

Since the tragic incident occurred in the French Concession Water and Electricity Workers' Strike, it has become increasingly serious. The number of strikers has reached more than a thousand, estimated to be 60-70% of the factory's employees. Yesterday, a reporter from this newspaper interviewed Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Bureau of Social Affairs, to inquire about the aftermath measures. His remarks are recorded as follows:

Mediation Ineffective: Since the French Concession Water and Electricity Workers' Strike occurred, the Bureau of Social Affairs has tried to mediate. The labor side put forward four demands, with the main condition being an increase of eight yuan per month for each person. The labor side cited the factory's use of funds to increase the salaries of a few employees as a pretext. However, the Bureau of Social Affairs twice invited representatives from both sides to the bureau for consultation, and the labor side arrived as scheduled, but the factory side has not sent anyone, so mediation has not been possible.

Arbitration Conference: According to the Labor Dispute Law, when the Bureau of Social Affairs cannot mediate, it should request the Municipal Government to convene a Labor-Capital Arbitration Committee meeting to resolve the issue. Therefore, the bureau has already submitted a request to the Municipal Government for handling last week and is currently conducting informal negotiations with the French Consul, etc., but there is no progress yet. The Labor-Capital Arbitration Conference will be convened after the negotiations are completed.

Reasons for Difficulties: The only reason why the resolution of this strike is slightly difficult is that the actual power of the factory is completely in the hands of the board of directors in Paris, and everything must be instructed and handled. The board of directors has a strong attitude, stating that they do not need to be subject to Chinese law, so the strike has become increasingly worse. Previously, Mr. Du Yuesheng had come forward in a private capacity to mediate, and the conditions had all been agreed upon. The strike could have been resolved, but the factory side suddenly and fundamentally overturned the agreement, leaving the intermediary helpless.

Final Method: Pan also said that if it is absolutely impossible to resolve the issue, it may be necessary to use diplomatic methods. However, they are currently making every effort to avoid this last resort. Furthermore, the factory also values its business and does not want this dispute to continue, so it is expected that there will be appropriate measures soon. The four water mains of the French Concession Water Company are all in the Chinese-controlled area and are being closely protected by the authorities, as is the water plant, in order to ensure that the residents of the French Concession do not suffer from a lack of drinking water, it is said.

Yesterday's News on the French Business Water and Electricity Workers' Strike

Municipal Party Committee Members Stationed at the Labor Union for Guidance

The Labor Union and Supporting Committee Sent a Letter to the French Consul

Party Committee Stationed: After the French business water and electricity workers' strike expanded, the situation became increasingly serious. In addition to telegraphing the central government and requesting the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to negotiate with the French ambassador, the Municipal Party Committee specially dispatched Committee Member Yang Qingyuan to Beijing to report the course of the labor strike and the truth of the tragedy, and to request instructions on how to handle the matter. The newspaper briefly reported these details yesterday. It is now learned that the Party Committee believes that the labor union should not be without leadership during the serious period of the labor strike. Therefore, it was decided that Comrade Hou Dachun should be stationed at the labor union to be responsible for guiding all progress.

Municipal Government Meeting: The Municipal Government specially convened a meeting yesterday morning, and representatives from the Municipal Party Committee also participated. Specific measures for the water and electricity workers' strike were discussed, and Secretary Geng was dispatched to the French Consul-General's Office to negotiate with the French Consul. It is reported that the results were extremely satisfactory.

Staff Meeting: The French Electric Company's Chinese Staff Support Committee held a meeting at 10:00 AM yesterday. More than a hundred staff members attended. The meeting proceeded as scheduled. Zhang Renjun was elected as the temporary chairman, and the purpose of the meeting was reported. Subsequently, eleven committee members were elected, namely Feng Zhiming, Feng Shenghuan, Zhang Renjun, Fan Baokun, Xu Tingliang, Xing Wenrong, Hu Zukun, Wang Liefan, Hu Yukang, Chen Hongyuan, and Lu Guanhong, to be responsible for carrying out the work. (2) A declaration should be issued. (3) Staff currently employed should be advised to resign as soon as possible to support the workers. (4) The staff should prepare to join the labor union to increase the strength of the group. (5) All members must attend the meeting at 9:00 AM every day.

Staff Strike Declaration: The company staff specially issued a declaration supporting the strike, stating: "The French water and electricity workers, driven by the necessities of life, have been forced to put forward extremely ordinary and appropriate demands, requesting the company to improve treatment in order to maintain their hard life. However, the management, adhering to its imperialist and oppressive tactics, resolutely refused and closed the iron gates, expelling the workers and forcing a strike that has lasted for more than thirty days. The Chinese authorities have been asked to mediate, but the management has no sincerity in accepting the mediation and disregards it. Furthermore, they have intensified their efforts by hiring White Russian new workers to work in the factory, which will leave hundreds of Chinese workers with no way to make a living, and ultimately led to the bloody tragedy on Malan Road on July 21, killing one Chinese person and wounding our apprentice workers with guns. When the bad news came, everyone was shocked and indignant. The staff members belong to the same compatriots and share the same fate. Seeing this crisis, how can we bear to sit idly by? Therefore, more than one hundred Chinese employees in the factory have united to leave the factory immediately, declare support, join the strike front, and fight together to urge the French imperialist capitalists to be sensible and secure the victory for our hundreds of workers. If the goal is not achieved, the strike will not end. This is our declaration, and we hope the public will take note."

Letter from Staff to Factory Management: "Dear Sirs, the fact that the workers in the Machinery Department and others are forced by livelihood to request the company to improve their treatment is due to the environment they are in. Moreover, the price of rice has risen recently, and the cost of living is increasing day by day, making it impossible for the workers to maintain their lives. As for the six demands of the workers, they are peaceful and moderate, and are not beyond the company's capabilities. Even if there are excessive points, they can be discussed calmly. Why should they be ignored, resulting in this strike? After the strike, although there have been several consultations, the company has not sincerely accepted them, and has disregarded the workers' lives. This action is extremely shocking and absurd. Up to now, more than thirty days have passed, and there is still no room for mediation, and the recent tragedy on Malan Road has been brewed. This is something that the staff cannot bear to sit idly by. In order to promote the company's awareness and to prevent both sides from moving to extremes, the staff has no choice but to temporarily suspend their duties to mediate for the workers, so as to avoid the expansion of the labor strike. Therefore, we specially write to request that the company resolve this unfortunate incident as soon as possible. If you are willing to accept our request and first dismiss the new workers and White Russians, so that the old workers can resume work as soon as possible, then the staff can also resume work as soon as possible. We would be extremely grateful and moved to tears. We respectfully submit this request and ask for your consideration."
